Therefore, he strongly advocated that Britain should continue its policy of international cooperation in the European continent under the banner of Geneva. The speech stated, "The United States is about 3,000 miles away from Europe, not like our Britain, which is within the range of continental artillery shells. I dare to assert that if Britain abandons its inherent beliefs and abolishes its international treaties, war will be imminent. If all kinds of guarantees for the welfare and security of other ethnic groups are recklessly abandoned, the result of this policy may inevitably lead the whole world to unite and arm against our country. Former Chancellor of the Exchequer Churchill once said that the main reason for European unrest is due to the current psychological state of Germany, and his words are true. All our people regard this psychology as harmful. However, the whole world knows that the Hitler regime has taken deep root, and I do not expect the overthrow of this regime. What we hope is that the Hitler regime will continue to develop and change its course, becoming a new spirit of peace, on which the security and interests of all nations depend." (Berlin) German leader Hitler attended the launching ceremony of the new ship "Scharnhorst" of the North German Company in White Rim and then took a fast train back to Beijing. No one was injured in the fast train. At that time, Hitler led the people to rescue the victims and helped to remove the debris on the track. He then comforted the injured one by one. Research on the Root of Sarcoma Is Due to a Compound 88

As Important as the Discovery of the Tuberculosis Bacillus

(New York) Dr. Wood, Director of the Sarcoma Research Institute at Columbia University and editor-in-chief of the Sarcoma Journal, explained the root of sarcoma and said that the root of sarcoma is a compound, and its discovery is as important as Dr. Koch's discovery of the tuberculosis bacillus in 1882. This compound was invented by Dr. Cook of the London Sarcoma Research Institute. Cook is a British chemist who has been funded by the International Sarcoma Research Foundation, which is donated by Donald of Philadelphia to encourage domestic and foreign scholars to research sarcoma. According to Dr. Cook's theory, there may be some life-sustaining substances, but for other reasons, they undergo chemical reactions to become sarcoma roots. (Kokumin dispatch from the 10th)

]H> Third sheet, eleventh edition

German Pocket Battleship 89

Another Method of Arms Race

Further Advancement of Scientific Competition

The preliminary naval talks in London involve only three naval powers: Great Britain, the United States, and Japan. People who pay attention to world issues and understand the situation in the Pacific can foresee what the future holds. Moreover, each country has its strengths. The British Navy occupies the throne of the seas, so its battleships are stronger than those of the United States and Japan. Although its cruisers under 10,000 tons are not as sophisticated as Japan's, they are numerous and have great organizational power. The United States excels in aircraft carriers. The "Lexington" is a converted battleship capable of carrying more than 80 aircraft, with a speed of 33 knots per hour, which is unmatched by Great Britain and Japan. Japan's submarines have almost the same hull design, and their attacking

effectiveness is more than twice as high as that of the German submarines used during the Great War.

In the past few years, the world's naval powers have been secretly competing, each showing their strengths. Germany is indeed a defeated country, but no one in the country has forgotten revenge or the task of revitalizing the nation. However, it is bound by the Treaty of Versailles, which allows the navy to have only 15,000 soldiers and warships only of the old "Deutschland" class, six ships. This is such a painful matter. Therefore, when Hitler raised his arms and called out, the people of Germany responded enthusiastically. Of course, Hitler was good at taking advantage of the environment and deeply understood the traditions of German history, but the strong and striving spirit of the German nation was also a key element.

The German Navy is severely restricted, unable to build warships or aircraft. So what should it do? In 1928, according to the treaty, it was allowed to build a new ship to replace the old "Deutschland." But there was still a restriction: the ship's tonnage could not exceed 10,000 tons, and the guns had to be below 11-inch caliber. The new "Deutschland," launched in 1931 and completed last year, is what is known as a pocket battleship.

Although this warship is small in tonnage and the guns are not large, it is the world's first solid and powerful warship. The first thing that deserves our attention is that each steel plate of the ship is joined without a single steel nail, but with the latest electrical welding method. This saves the weight of the hull for loading weapons, and the saved weight is 550 tons. The second is the installation of eight diesel engines, each with 7,100 horsepower, totaling 56,800 horsepower for the entire ship, which is light and agile. Third, it is equipped with 11-inch caliber guns. Needless to say, these guns are made of first-class steel from Germany's top steel factory, Krupp Steel. The gun barrels are much longer than ordinary 11-inch guns. Each shell weighs 670 pounds. Seeing that the gun barrel is longer than ordinary guns, we know that the initial velocity of the shell is very high. The range of the shell is 27,800 meters, and the elevation angle is 60 degrees. These three points are unprecedented achievements for modern warships of various powers.

Another point, which is rare in modern ordinary warships, is that the central part of the ship is covered with armored steel plates, and the upper deck is also divided into two layers, with air defense equipment. The ship's maximum speed is 26 knots. If it maintains a speed of 20 knots, its endurance can be 10,000 nautical miles. It can travel from Shanghai to Seattle and back without refueling. This is truly a pocket ship.

The ship is 606 feet long, 67.5 feet wide, and has a draft of 21.5 feet. It carries six 11-inch guns, eight 6-inch guns, four 3.4-inch anti-aircraft guns, and six 19.7-inch torpedoes. The sharpness of these weapons is no less than that of a 20,000-ton warship. No wonder the world is surprised, considering it a new record in the creation of weapons. The construction of this warship cost £3.75 million (if each pound is calculated at 16 yuan, it is worth 60 million Chinese silver dollars). In addition to the sister ship "Admiral Scheer," which can be completed this year, there are two more under construction. Germany's current finances are in a period of extreme difficulty, and foreign trade is not improving. However, it is still striving to move upward, insisting on equality of armaments on the one hand and striving to establish considerable armaments on the other, with science as its backing, giving full play to its organizational power. Although the future is not optimistic, its efforts to move upward are indeed worthy of our admiration. (Berlin, November 8)

The Japanese Threat Recently Felt by the Philippines 90

U.S. Commissioner Advocates Continued U.S. Protection for 25 Years

— By Wen Chu

Japan has always advocated a policy of southward and northward expansion. The northward expansion is to invade the mainland by force, and the southward expansion is to invade the South Seas economically. Although the northward expansion has achieved a large part of its goals and is still in full swing, the southward expansion is not relaxed because of this. Therefore, the dumping of Japanese goods in various Dutch and British colonies has recently caused conflicts between Britain and Japan, and there have been many conflicts between Japan and the Netherlands. The Philippines is a part of the South Seas, and its current master is the United States, which is very close to Japan. Since the situation in the Pacific has become increasingly tense, Japan has been making more efforts in military and economic terms. Therefore, since the United States established the Philippine Independence Act ten years later, those Filipinos with great vision have been pessimistic, fearing that it will become the second Manchuria in the future. However, what is the actual strength of Japan in the Philippines? This should also be what those who care about Eastern issues want to know. Please briefly describe the outline as follows:

Thirty years ago, there were very few Japanese people in the Philippines. Apart from the life of a small trader, there was no other achievement. At that time, the United States had just taken over the Philippines, and there was a place called Davao in the south, which was sparsely populated. The government allowed people to claim land for reclamation. In 1904, a Japanese named Ota Kyosaburo came here to run a small business and knew that planting was promising in this area. So he went to Taiwan to make friends with the authorities and offered the plan of cultivating Davao to the Governor-General of Taiwan. The Governor-General thought it was feasible and invested one million as capital. Many nobles and wealthy merchants also joined. Ota then came to Davao with the capital and established the Ota Industrial Co., Ltd. for large-scale cultivation. From then on, he reclaimed wasteland, built roads and water conservancy projects, and built wharves. Japanese farmers and workers continued to come, with hemp as their main business. The planting and stripping were done using scientific methods, so the product's fiber was tough, long, and white, which was the best in the Philippines. They were all transported to Japanese factories, made into hemp fabrics, and then imported back to the Philippines for sale. Davao is now a trading port. Every week, large Japanese ships come and go directly. Initially, Chinese and Japanese immigrants had the same regulations in the Philippine government. Later, because of their country's wealth and strength, the government treated them as equals to Europeans and Americans (the so-called immigration law was to crack down on the people of China, India, and Korea). Farmers, businessmen, and workers could travel through the islands with just a letter of introduction from the Japanese consul, without having to go through immigration bureau investigations or pay 20 yuan in stamp fees for a residence permit, with Davao as their base camp. Therefore, in the Japanese residential area in Davao, there are schools, hospitals, and other organizations. In addition to the Ota Company, there is also the Furukawa Company, which is also very large in scale. Davao has now become a Japanese world. According to the Japanese consul's announcement, its population accounts for two-thirds of the Japanese in the islands. Also, the Philippine Congress passed a law in 1919 stating that foreigners could not own land in the Philippines. According to the Japanese consul's announcement, the Japanese in Davao only purchased 2,500 hectares of land, all of which were legally purchased before 1919. However, at the opening of the Philippine Constitutional Convention this year, the representative of Davao Province gave a public speech, revealing the inside story of Japanese land purchases in the province, saying that the provincial authorities had allowed the Japanese in the area to develop real estate without seeking relief. The upper class figures in Davao often bought land from the government and then resold it to the Japanese in the area. Since this report was issued, Philippine newspapers have published warning news, arousing the attention of Filipinos. Unexpectedly, not long after, there was another case of smuggling arms.

After the Davao district representative exposed the inside story of land purchases, the representative of the Mindanao Province (adjacent to Davao) made a more important report, saying that he had received secret information that the Japanese were smuggling arms into Davao on Japanese ships and hiding them in Japanese tombs. This issue is even more serious, because the Japanese intention is to make Davao a military hypothetical base. For the future Japanese-American war, there is a great threat, which has aroused great attention from the American and Philippine authorities.

Not only that, the intrusion of Japanese fishing boats into Philippine territorial waters is also common. Sometimes, the theft of maps is also discovered. The Philippine authorities have no way to investigate deeply. Recently, it was discovered that the Japanese fishing boat Haiyang Maru in Palawan (a southern province) was smuggling explosives and contraband. Military police boarded the ship to search, and the sailors of the ship shot and killed the military police and threw the body into the sea. The ship sped off to Taiwan. Although the Philippine customs dispatched four cruisers to pursue, they were not found. The Philippine government wanted to continue the extradition according to law, but the Taiwanese Japanese authorities and the Tokyo press refused extradition, expressing a tough attitude. The Philippine government also has no judicial disposition, and will only become a pending case in the future.

As for the commercial power of the two countries in the Philippines, Japan has made rapid progress compared to the United States. According to the announcement of the U.S. Department of Commerce, in 1932, the total imports of the Philippines were 159.79 million yuan, of which U.S. goods were 102.98 million, accounting for about 65%. In 1933, the total imports of the Philippines were 149.36 million yuan, of which U.S. goods were 87.57 million, accounting for about 59%. In 1932, Japanese goods imported into the Philippines were only 9.45 million yuan. In 1933, it increased to 19.13 million yuan, an increase of more than 50% in one year, which has revealed its trend of replacing U.S. goods. Now the Philippines has not yet broken away from the U.S. relationship, and Japan's actions are already like this. Then, who knows that the so-called guarantee of Philippine independence will not repeat the old tune of annexing Korea and occupying the Northeast after independence, and say that in order to maintain peace in East Asia, the Philippines must be placed under its sphere of influence? Therefore, it has aroused the self-endangerment of the Filipinos. Therefore, the Philippine Resident Commissioner to the United States, Mr. Nitta, when he went to the United States last month to take office, made a statement to the "Armed Town" reporter of the U.S. newspaper in the Philippines, advocating that the Philippines should continue to rely on the protection of the United States for the next 25 years. He also spoke in the United States on the 24th of this month, saying that "Filipinos fear Japan and their security depends on the continued protection of the United States." Many people in the Philippine business community and other circles have also begun to move, and will submit a petition to the U.S. Congressional delegation that will arrive in the Philippines next month, requesting the U.S. Congress to extend the ten-year transition period of the Tydings-McDuffie Independence Act (the Philippine Independence Act proposed by U.S. congressmen) to twenty years. The Philippine Congress's immediate independence faction has not dared to express its opinions on the above proposal, which also shows the depth of fear of Japan. (Minila, the capital of the Philippine Islands, November 30)

Northwest Inspection Notes

— Special Correspondent Geng Ya of this Newspaper

The Water Conservancy of Xinjiang's "Karez" 91

On the 17th, we departed from Yandun, passed through the Yidao post station. The strata on both banks are seven or eight feet thick, with yellow sand on top and red soil below, the two not mixing together. Looking to the right, the Tianshan Mountains are dazzling with snow. Gazing at the Gobi Desert, the scenery is ever-changing. After more than ten miles, the road splits into two. The south leads to Chang Liushui, which is the main road, and the north leads to Hui Zhuangzi, which is a small road. Both places are sixty miles east of Yandun. However, Hui Zhuangzi has lush grasslands, which are far better than Chang Liushui. We traveled north to Tielejiang in order to fully feed the horses. After twenty miles, we crossed a black sand dry river. To the east, the Gobi Desert stretches as far as the eye can see. To the west, reeds cover the field, and clusters of red willow and white poplar are every few steps. More than ten riders gallop among them, unable to see the beginning or the end. The lushness of the vegetation can be imagined. Twenty miles to Hui Zhuangzi, there are two or three earthen houses, clear streams winding around, willow and apricot trees lining the road, and fertile fields of about one hundred and several tens of acres. Only one farmer lives there, but his resources are insufficient, and most of the land is barren. Twenty miles to the south, there are more than twenty white poplar trees and four or five farming families. This is Chang Liushui. Only because the land is flat and the air is fresh (thin and with less vapor), the two places, although twenty miles apart, seem as close as next door. Several tens of miles to the southwest, there are more faint village trees. The beauty of the scenery is the best since coming to Andunxi.

Before the sun had set completely in the west, the crowd decided to continue. The soil we were traveling on was soft and fertile, suitable for cultivation. The abundant grass we saw was deep enough to submerge the riders. Three or five horses grazing among the reeds were fattening up in the autumn. Their loud neighing often startled passersby. Thirty miles to Liu Jia Zhuangzi, and ten miles further west is Kekeyi Well, hence this place is also known as Kekeyi Well. We took off the saddles, released the horses, and stayed there. The weather was warm, and we only needed a lined jacket. I remembered that when we passed Malian Well before, heavy fur coats were not warm enough. Now we have entered a warm land, as if coming from a cold zone. A few days ago, in order to avoid the shopkeeper's insistence on eating half-raw meat, horse sausage, and mutton that had been slaughtered for a long time, I pretended to have a toothache, still fearing that people would not believe me. Later, because the weather changed drastically, with one day of cold and heat like two zones, and also because of the fatigue of riding, the fire in my body easily rose, causing my left tooth to really become painful. It can be said that "ask and you shall receive."

There is an earthen house in Liu Jia Zhuang. Entering the walled gate, the courtyard is covered with a grass shed, enclosing a stone mill. The house is divided into two rooms, one for storing food and vegetables, and the other for the tenant farmer to live in. The tenant farmer is a Hui farmer, so the interior arrangement is different. The back part of the room is a kang, occupying about two-thirds of the entire room, about seven or eight inches higher than the original ground. It is covered with felt blankets and used for all kinds of work, eating, and drinking. At night, the bedding is spread out for sleeping, and in the morning, the bedding is piled in the wall cabinet or in the left corner behind the kang, covered with a floral curtain, which looks neat and tidy. In the right front corner of the kang, a stove is built against the wall, level with the kang. The stove hole is dug deep underground, and when burning firewood, one squats inside the kang and curves a groove under the kang, so that the kang is heated when cooking. In the left front corner of the kang, another stove is built against the wall, and the smoke passes through the roof. Its style is exactly the same as the fireplace used in Western buildings, except that the former is made of earth and the latter is made of metal. History says that ancient Western European culture was mostly transmitted from Central Asia. Now, seeing the wall stove can be used as evidence. The Hui woman and her three or four daughters all wear melon-skin caps woven with thread, colored in five colors, but without a top knot. Those who are married wear long braids hanging down their backs, and those who are not married wear three or four braids each, without a fixed number. They wear red cloth long skirts and short jackets, and their bare feet wear boots like men's. The mother and daughters look like sisters, with an age difference of only fourteen years. This is because the Hui custom values early marriage. Girls marry as early as thirteen or fourteen years old and can have children early. Outside the walled gate, there are two large deep pits, obliquely dug with earthen steps to connect the top and bottom. One is covered with an earthen roof, called the "Underground Cellar Room," which is warm in winter and cool in summer, and is still used for living. The other has no roof, called the "Open-air Stable," which is blocked by wooden steps and can hold livestock. A little further away, there is another circular earthen stove, about three feet high, shaped like a kiln, like a skin-smoking stove, called the "Naan Pit," which is used for baking dough. Its function is quite similar to a steamer. The method is to first burn firewood and grass, making it into ashes and charcoal. The inner edge of the pit is red hot, and then the prepared dough is placed one by one on the side, covering the opening for a moment, and it will immediately turn yellow and cooked, with a crisp texture and fragrant taste. Its name is "Naan." This is the main food of the Hui people. Other things, such as roasted meat, which must be used to entertain guests, are also mostly roasted in the Naan pit.

The village land is sixty square miles, and the same land has been opened for cultivation for seven years. The white poplar and green apricot trees that have been cultivated are only as thick as a handful, slender and lush, and very lovable. The area of ​​Hami County is about 200,000 square miles, and the arable land is less than 1%. As for the remaining 99%, the coarse sand Gobi Desert cannot be cultivated. As for the fine sand grassland, as long as the water source problem is solved, there is nothing that cannot be cultivated. To solve the water source problem, it is impossible to divert the snow water of the Tianshan Mountains or the river water. The only way is to dig "Karez" (see attached pictures). The barren mountains and wastelands of Hami were originally controlled by "Wangye." After repeated negotiations with the provincial government, they have gradually been opened up in recent years. If the people want to cultivate a certain land, they must first register with the county government, and then dig a "Karez" to obtain water. The county government will then issue a license. They will plant for the first three years and be exempt from paying grain tax. From the fourth year onwards, they must pay the grain tax according to the amount. For a time, those who applied for reclamation were very enthusiastic. However, due to the difficulty of obtaining water from the "Karez" and the occurrence of the incident twenty years ago, the result of this reclamation was not very significant. According to Liu Yuanxiao, the owner of Wang Jia Zhuang, "The success of cultivation here means that all kinds of grains are suitable for cultivation. On average, one stone of wheat seed can yield eleven stones of wheat. According to this year's grain price, each stone of wheat weighs 400 catties and is worth about 16 yuan. Eleven stones are worth a total of 176 yuan. After deducting the official grain of three dou, which is equivalent to 4.8 yuan, the seed one stone of 16 yuan, the cattle labor four frames totaling 4 yuan, the labor 40 totaling 8 yuan, plus miscellaneous expenses of several yuan, the total expenditure is about 40 yuan. After deducting the expenditure, each stone of land can obtain a net profit of more than 130 yuan. No fertilizer is applied to the land. Each year, one-third of the planting is rotated, and the remaining two-thirds are plowed and dried for two years, which is as effective as applying fertilizer. Twenty years ago, a Hui rebellion occurred, and they dared not return to cultivate the land themselves. Therefore, they rented it out to Hui farmers according to the equal division method. Many other Han Chinese farmland are also handled in this way." This shows that Hami is sparsely populated, the soil is fertile, and the tax is light. If the leadership and management are effective, the agricultural future is indeed promising.

I don't know when the Xinjiang "Karez" was created, but since Lin Zexu came to Xinjiang, he vigorously promoted it, and it began to spread to various places and achieved results. The digging method of "Karez" is roughly as shown in the attached figure. First, dig a ditch in a low and humid place, which is level with the ground. Initially, it is called the "Tunnel Entrance" (as shown in Figure A). The tunnel is five feet high and two feet wide, which is convenient for digging sand and soil, and also convenient for the outflow of well water. At the same time, from the ground, along the line that the tunnel wants to pass through, wells are dug every five or six zhang (as shown in Figure D) in order to connect with the "Tunnel Ditch" (as shown in Figure AO connecting line). This is to ventilate and take sand, and to facilitate

Page 12

future repairs. The well is initially seven or eight feet deep, and later, due to the gradually rising ground, it is as deep as six or seven zhang (the Karez in Turpan is as deep as thirty or forty zhang). All are dug to the groundwater line (as shown in Figure AO connecting line). The wells are connected to form a huge flow, gushing out continuously throughout the four seasons (as shown in the arrow). Each "Karez" has dozens or even hundreds of wells, and the tunnel ditch is more than ten miles long. Digging it is a real waste of manpower. Digging but not getting water is called "White Karez." The custom uses "White Karez" to refer to things that are laborious but fruitless, or to people who are useless. The meaning is based on this. The wellhead must be properly sealed, and the tunnel entrance must be blocked in winter to prevent cold air from flowing in, freezing and collapsing. However, the rushing water flow can still be allowed to go out.

Tang Yulin's Lawsuit with Former Subordinates 92

Accused His Chief of Military Supplies at the Military Branch

Alleging Embezzlement of 500,000 Yuan in Military Uniform Expenses

Tianjin communication, after Tang Yulin lost power, his children, grandchildren, and other descendants mostly lived in peace and affluence in Pingjin. However, when Tang was in power, the province of Rehe was his family's world. His nephews and nieces relied on their power to be tyrannical and did many unjust things, making enemies with many people. Once their feathers were hidden, those who had been bullied by them in the past took the opportunity to rise up and thought of revenge. As a result, the Tang family has been involved in numerous lawsuits. The Tianjin court has accepted cases such as Tang Yulin's divorce from his concubine, Ms. Hu, Tang's eldest son, Zuo Rong's embezzlement of Rehe Lama's scriptures, embezzlement of antiquities from the Lama Temple, divorce from his concubines, Ms. Zhao and Ms. Zhang, (Tang Yulin's) grandson's divorce from his daughter-in-law, and (Tang Yulin's) daughter's elopement with Jiang Jing. These cases have made Tianjin chaotic. After more than a year, three or five have been decided after legal sanctions, and some are still undecided, such as Tang Zuo Rong's embezzlement of antiquities from the Rehe Lama Temple. The Tianjin Land Inspection Office is investigating the evidence and has not yet finished the hearing. The other is Tang Zuo Fu's embezzlement case. This matter is slightly more dignified than the other Tang family lawsuits. Tang Yulin has recently submitted a petition to the Beiping Military Branch, requesting a military trial. The incident has gradually expanded and become heated. The outline is as follows: When Tang Yulin was the commander of the Rehe Border Defense, his son Zuo Fu was the Director of Finance. Zuo Fu was greedy for money and goods. He found out that Liu Baoqing, the Chief of Military Supplies of the Rehe Border Defense Command, had embezzled 500,000 yuan in military uniform expenses. Tang Zuo Fu planned to split the money, but Liu refused. Zuo Fu then reported it to his father and had Liu arrested and imprisoned. At the same time, Zuo Fu, together with Huang Jinbiao, the adjutant of the Border Defense Command, Tan Yufu, the captain of the motorcade, and his concubine Jin Ziling, came to Tianjin and stayed in their house on Sanma Road in the Italian Concession. They tricked Liu Baoqing's mother, Liu's brother Bao Fu, and many other relatives into being privately imprisoned in their Italian Concession house, where they were tortured and forced to sign evidence of the transfer of all their property. Only after Liu Bao Fu and his mother signed the promise were they released. After Liu's mother returned home, she fell ill with fright and died. The Liu family's property, worth hundreds of thousands, was transferred to Tang's hands. When Rehe fell, Liu Baoqing escaped and returned to Tianjin. Last year, he sued Zuo Fu in the Tianjin court for embezzling property, illegal imprisonment, and other crimes. After several trials, Zuo Fu denied that he had ever come to Tianjin, saying that the matter existed, but it was done by Huang Jinbiao, Tan Yufu, and others under the orders of their superiors and had nothing to do with him. He also said that Liu Baoqing was able to become the Chief of Military Supplies because Liu set up a brothel at the Shenyang West Station. When Tang was prostituting, he met Liu's father and, through various relationships, was able to be appointed as a confidant. His family property was accumulated from embezzling public funds over the years. The court held that even if these things were true, they were not enough to defend the case. Therefore, the result of the first trial was that Tang was sentenced to three years and six months in prison, his concubine Jin Ziling was sentenced to eight months in prison, and Tan Yufu, the captain of the motorcade, was sentenced to three years and six months in prison, all in prison. This spring, Tan Yufu died in prison. Zuo Fu and his concubine refused to accept the first-instance judgment and appealed to the High Court, and requested a transfer of jurisdiction, which was not permitted. The High Court conducted the first hearing on the 11th of this month, and the most detailed investigation was made on whether Tang Zuo Fu and his concubine Jin Ziling came to Tianjin that day. Zuo Fu is addicted to opium and committed opium crimes once with his concubine in prison. Later, he repeatedly requested bail for illness, but was not allowed. Therefore, he hated Liu Baoqing very much. In order to rescue his son, Tang Yulin specially submitted a petition to the Ping Military Branch, accusing Liu Baoqing of embezzling more than 500,000 yuan in military uniform expenses during his tenure as Chief of Military Supplies, which involved military matters. Therefore, he requested a subpoena for trial. The Military Branch then sent the leader of the eleventh group to Tianjin to investigate with the court a few days ago. Therefore, this case may be transferred to the Ping Military Branch for adjudication. (12th)

Purple Cloud Cave Adventure in Hangzhou 93

Zhejiang National Military Training Association Organizes a Team to Explore

Sensational Throughout the City, Tourists Flock

Hangzhou Dispatch: Jade Emperor Mountain in the south of the city towers into the clouds. During the severe drought this summer, Zhang Tianshi (a Daoist master) planned to perform rituals there, but it did not materialize. Halfway up the mountain is the ancient Purple Cloud Cave, rumored to extend to Huizhou. Previously, it was covered in overgrown weeds and mist, obscuring the cave entrance. Although pilgrims flocked to the mountain peak, no one had ever explored its depths. Last month, the Hangzhou YMCA initiated an exploration, but it failed to complete the task due to insufficient preparations. On the 9th of this month, Xiao Zuguang, Gu Yiming, Yu Wuqing, Chen Jiayu, Lin Heng, and others from the Zhejiang National Military Training Association, along with He Wengan, Luo Xine, Hu Bosun, Sun Daoren, and more than ten others from the Hangzhou National New Society, organized a Purple Cloud Cave exploration team with the intention of breaking superstitions and inspiring a spirit of national adventure. Each member carried a strong flashlight, as well as ropes, knives, self-defense pistols, hemp ropes, wooden sticks, tape measures, compasses, cameras, and other self-defense equipment. They also prepared a commemorative wooden plaque with the signatures of all the team members. At 10 a.m. on the 9th, they ascended the mountain. After reaching the cave entrance, each team member took off their long coats and tied the rope end to a stone. He Wengan and Luo Xine led the way into the cave, immediately stooping to enter the tunnel, which sloped westward at an angle of about forty degrees to the horizontal. They advanced more than twenty fathoms.

The Cave Passage Narrows, Barely Enough Room to Pass 94

They continued to advance diagonally downward for another forty fathoms, then turned south. The walls were slightly wider than before, creating a sloping area that could accommodate more than ten people. By this time, all one hundred fathoms of hemp rope tied to the cave entrance had been used. They struck the rocks with stones and then crept forward again. After another twenty fathoms, the cave passage dropped straight down, forming a ninety-degree angle with the horizontal. Shining a thousand-foot-strong flashlight down, they peered over the edge, facing an abyss. The light could not reach the bottom.

Jagged Stone Walls, A Gaping Mountain Root 95

Subsequently, on the right side of the rock face, they discovered a crack that could be climbed up and down. Each of them untied one end of the five-fathom-long hemp rope they were carrying, secured it to the rock crevice, and lowered the other end from the cave entrance. First, Luo Xine descended along the rope, carrying a pistol and the wooden plaque. At the bottom of the rope, he shone the flashlight down and saw a protruding rock that could be used as a foothold. He then leaped down the cliff. The electric torch illuminated a space of about one square fathom. The rock walls were like...

Layers of Clouds and Accumulated Rain, Resembling Strange Beasts 96

The bottom of the cave was as flat as water, formed purely of accumulated fine mud. He Wengan jokingly fired his gun into the ground, and the bullet entered the soil with a "whoosh" sound. They also discovered a stone tube standing upright to the northwest, which could still be climbed by hugging the wall. He Wengan...

He Wengan and Luo Xine, carrying the commemorative plaque, wearing shorts, and barefoot, clung to the wall and ascended. First, they pressed their backs against the east side of the cave, with their feet against the opposite rock wall, wriggling their muscles, inch by inch. Although...

Limbs Trembling, Soul and Courage Shattered 97

Their ambition drove them to reach the very end. After about six fathoms, they found a place to stand on the west side of the rock wall. Shining the light upwards, they saw stalactites hanging down from the top and two pairs of bats perched there. He and Luo used small knives to carve off a piece of strange rock and placed the commemorative plaque on a stone "chair." They then climbed back down the wall and took a photo with their companions in the cave. Because they did not bring magnesium flash, the image was blurry. They agreed to follow the original route and climb out of the cave using the rope. There were dozens of onlookers at the cave entrance, lighting candles and applauding their success. By then, it was 6:40 p.m. The team later...

Announces the Experience, Rewards Adventure 98

Said that anyone who could retrieve the commemorative plaque would be awarded a one-year subscription to the Hangzhou National News. After the news spread, Zhou Zhaohua, a skilled athlete from Guangdong, and others entered the cave the next day, retrieved the commemorative plaque, and captured a pair of bats. The National News Agency has begun to provide daily subscriptions. Xu Shilong and others from the Zhejiang Automobile Company also brought batteries, wires, and electric cannons. Others carrying knives and sticks in groups of three or five flocked to the path. The military training association exploration team, fearing that the crowds of tourists would inevitably lead to accidental falls and injuries, braved the stars and dew at 11 p.m. on the 13th and entered the cave at midnight.

Splitting Rocks and Building Wooden Structures to Benefit Tourists 99

They also found a photograph of Zhou Zhaohua and others on the top of the cave. According to an old Daoist priest living on the mountain, the previous time, Westerners from the Meifu (Mobil) Company had climbed down the wall but were unable to climb back up. Fortunately, their police dog came out of the cave and signaled to the Daoist, who rescued them with a white cloth. Seven sets of corpses were found at the bottom of the cave and have been buried. Breaking through the rocky cave was something no one had done before.

Songjiang Rifeng Silver Shop Claims Robbery 100

Recently, robbery cases have occurred frequently in the city, and local people feel alarmed. They are planning to handle winter defense to deter bandits. Unexpectedly, at 9 a.m. this morning (the 15th), at the Rifeng Silver Shop in Fengle Bridge in the city, a young man in a Western suit carried out a robbery under the guise of purchasing gold bracelets. The shopkeeper, Zhao Houzhuang, from Shaoxing, aged 64, seeing that the man looked suspicious, tried to snatch back the gold bracelet. The young man in the Western suit shot him with a pistol, the bullet entering his left chest and exiting his right chest. The young man handed the gold bracelet, weighing more than one tael, to an accomplice who was keeping watch, and they fled the city across the Shuiguan Bridge together. The guard police chased after them and telegraphed the Public Security Bureau to have the security team surround and arrest them. A large number of armed police were dispatched to pursue them. As a result, a pistol and a dagger were seized by the water patrol team near the Yang Bridge at No. 22 Zhongpanlongtang Railway outside the East Gate. A student certificate from the Xu Hui Public School was also found. The team leader interrogated him. According to his confession, his name was Zhao Zhiyi, 21 years old, from Changmen, Suzhou. He was married to a daughter of Yang Yengeng in this city. His father worked for the Shanghai Public Security Bureau. He directly admitted that he and a Qiu surnamed man from Suzhou, who worked as a partner in a sauce garden, had robbed the Rifeng Bank together. The original stolen item was taken away by Qiu, who was on the run. The Water Patrol Team and the Public Security Bureau jointly searched for the fleeing Qiu and searched the sauce garden, but found no evidence. The captured Zhao Zhiyi was temporarily detained pending dispatch to the county for investigation. The injured Rifeng Bank assistant, Zhao Houzhuang, was taken to Songjiang Hospital for treatment. It is said that he is old and weak. If he does not develop a fever, his life may be safe. Currently, people from all walks of life in the area are concerned that robberies have occurred in prosperous urban areas, causing concerns about public security.

Baoshan Elementary Schools Hold Etiquette and Conduct Assessment Conference 101

The Jiangsu Province Elementary School Student Etiquette and Conduct Assessment Conference was scheduled by the province to be held uniformly on November 12. However, it rained on that day and could not be held. Baoshan originally rescheduled it for November 18, but it rained again on that day. It was then rescheduled for yesterday (the 14th) at the Baoshan City District Public Sports Field. Twenty-one schools, including Qianxi, Guizhai, Songyang, and Luoyang, participated on that day. The chairman was County Magistrate Long Tiyao. The inspector was County Magistrate Long Tiyao. The director of the Education Bureau was Xu Zejun. The judges were Zhu Xuedian, a special commissioner of the county party headquarters, Wang Xiusan, secretary of the county government, Pu Jiying, principal of the county junior high school, Jin Shuwen, a local gentleman, and various education commissioners. The assessment results were: first place, Baisha Elementary School; second place, Songyang Elementary School; third place, Chengzhong Elementary School, Zixi Elementary School.

Jiading Police Officer Who Fled with Weapon Apprehended and Returned to the County 102

Sha Younan, a first-class police officer from the No. 1 Branch of the Nanxiang Public Security Substation, Hefei County, Anhui Province, recently fled from his post with a No. 3 Browning pistol and thirty bullets. The Public Security Bureau Chief, Chen Youmin, recorded a major demerit for Cao Hanqing, the supervising patrolman in charge, and ordered him to pursue and arrest Sha, and the case was reported to the county government to request the Civil Affairs Department to issue an arrest warrant. Cao Xun promptly sent police to Nantong to track him down, based on a tip-off that the fugitive police officer lived in Nantong. He was arrested and brought back to the county government for investigation.

Senmao Silk Shop Announces Liquidation 103

Senmao Silk Shop on East Avenue is an old shop with more than 70 years of history. The shop owner, Zhu Zunlin, has held important positions in the Chamber of Commerce. In recent years, due to repeated famines and wars in the region, business has been slow and funds have not been circulating smoothly. Starting from the 13th, he has suspended business and entrusted lawyer Zhang Tianbai to announce the liquidation. It is said that only one item remains: a huge sum of 50,000 to 60,000 gold.

Changshu Leader of the High Collar Gang Arrested 104

The county has long had a secret organization called the High Collar Gang, which specializes in making trouble, turning falsehoods into reality, and engaging in various base and violent acts such as gathering crowds to beat people. The beating of Ge Renyuan, director of the Education Bureau, in the spring was done by them. The gang members are scattered in various places, and if their wishes are not met, disaster will strike immediately. Recently, the gang members started an internal conflict due to uneven distribution of spoils. Four gang members, Zong Qichang, Cai Yushan, and Zhang Yongnian, published a notice in the newspaper to leave the gang and demanded that the gang leader, Li Kunwu, return their membership cards. This attracted the attention of the authorities, who are investigating and arresting them. Suddenly, they received a tip. The county party headquarters summoned the four who had published the notice and interrogated them. On the afternoon of the 14th, the party committee, Shi Minyong, secretly sent a letter to the county government, and together with the Public Security Bureau and a forensic doctor, searched Li Kunwu's home in Shuyuan Lane. Li Kunwu happened to be home and was immediately arrested. The articles of association of the Yiyou Mutual Aid Society, membership cards, and the complete case file of the analysis of the assets of the wealthy merchant brothers, Yang Zhanghang, were found. They were immediately taken to the bureau and transferred to the county judiciary for interrogation.

National Goods Mobile Exhibition Opens 105

The mobile exhibition organized by the Shanghai National Goods Factory Association has been exhibiting and promoting national goods everywhere. The mobile exhibition arrived in Chang on the 12th and is being held at the old Chenghuang Temple in front of the temple. Preparations have been completed. More than forty factories are coming to Chang with their products. The official opening is scheduled for the 15th. A banquet will be held for people from all walks of life on that day, and a grand lantern festival is planned. The exhibition will last for three weeks.

Suzhou Clam Mountain Massacre Bodies, Court to Inspect Today 106

Clam Mountain in Yangcheng River, a historically notorious bandit den, saw an unprecedented massacre. The corpses have been excavated by the Detective Team of the Water Public Security Bureau. The Wuxian District Court has scheduled a prosecutor to inspect the bodies today (the 16th).

Opening a Large-Scale National Goods Market 107

For the sake of promoting domestic goods, local resident Liu Zhengkang has raised 150,000 yuan to build a large-scale national goods market in the Beiju area of the city. The construction of the buildings has been completed. The market has decided to open a market on the ground floor and hotels or entertainment venues on the second and third floors. It is expected to open in February.

City Defense Amidst Robbery Reports 108

Since the beginning of winter, robberies have been frequently reported in various parts of Suzhou. Zhang Jinbang and other seven bandits captured by the Detective Team of the No. 2 Water Public Security District a few days ago are highly suspected of involvement in the robbery case at the home of Tang Shichang in Ximachi. The district headquarters notified Tang, and on the 15th, he sent personnel to identify them. Because the robbery took place at night and the faces were blurry, they could not be identified. The investigation is ongoing. The case of the Machengji Tu Gao shop at No. 52 Bifengfang Lane in the city has not yet been solved. County Magistrate Wu is paying close attention to this case. He ordered the Public Security Bureau yesterday to solve the case within three days. Zhang Hanwei, director of the Public Security Bureau, is concerned that the continuous robberies in the city are a matter of local security. Yesterday, he and the security team, Nie, met to discuss district defense. At that time, it was decided that the Public Security Bureau and the security team would send officers to station at the city gates and at wharves and vehicle stations to inspect suspicious passengers at any time. This will be implemented today (the 16th). At the same time, a proposal was submitted to the County Political Conference to organize a joint military-police inspection office to maintain local security.

Changzhou Majishan Embankment Project Completed 109

Majishan in the 10th District of Wu County was planned as a scenic area by former County Magistrate Cai Peijian. Because the area is surrounded by lakes on three sides and borders land on one side, the scenery is beautiful, but the more than 7,000 mu of land there is often flooded by the lake, resulting in poor harvests. In February of this year, local gentlemen Zhuang Zhongxi and Qian Linshu and others organized a committee to raise funds for building embankments and sluice gates. The funds were set at more than 20,000 yuan, which were temporarily advanced by the relief agency, the impoverished children's hospital, and the estate management office. After the project is completed, the benefited fields will repay the funds in three years. Construction began in early March. After more than eight months, the project has been completed. The embankment is twelve miles long, with three large sluice gates in the middle to regulate the water flow. As a result, this year's harvest is very good. District Chief Liao Zhigui reported the completion of the embankment project to the county government. The county magistrate, in addition to commissioning the Public Security Bureau Chief Xu Baoguang to inspect and accept the project, also scheduled to take the Wuyi Road long-distance bus to Xueyanqiao at 7 a.m. today (the 15th) with Wang Chao from the County Party Headquarters and others, hire a boat to Majishan to personally inspect and accept the project, and inspect the Baojia situation along the way.

Jiangyin Tobacco Control Investigator Comes to Cheng 110

The entire group of more than 80 students from the Provincial Tobacco Control Committee Investigator Training Class, after completing their training period, were divided into 12 groups and assigned to serve in various counties, adopting a guerrilla inspection method. Li Gongfu was assigned to Jiangyin, and on the 13th, he met with Zhang Xiabu, the newly appointed secretary, at the County Tobacco Control Association. He then dispatched investigator Xie Jian to inspect the rehabilitation center and then went to various sales points to investigate the daily sales volume of opium. At the Xinsheng Sales and Smoking Center on Hongqiao Riverbank, because the number of opium paste sales did not match and extra licenses were discovered, the contractor, Li Kunrong, was handed over to the Public Security Bureau for detention, pending interrogation by the Tobacco Control Association.

Wuxi Appoints Committee to Investigate Accounts of Past County Magistrates 111

Zhao Dihua, Director of the Jiangsu Department of Finance, recently stated that there are many cases of county magistrates whose accounts have not been cleared. It is necessary to investigate and set a deadline for submission. At the same time, County Magistrate Yan Shenyu of this county also reported that the accounts of past county magistrates and directors of the finance bureau have not been cleared. Therefore, he specially requested that a committee be appointed to investigate. Director Zhao then ordered Zhang Hesheng to come to Wuxi and be stationed in the county for investigation. It has now been found that the accounts of the previous county magistrates Zhang Hougu, Lin Fuozhen, Yang Tianji, and the county magistrates Yu Fu, Yu Liu, Kong Xiankeng, and ten other appointments have not been cleared. Among them, Zhang's losses are the greatest, totaling more than 10,000 yuan. Yang's losses are more than 3,000 yuan, and Lin's losses are the least, only 27 yuan. The cases have been reported to the department for verification and recovery. Former County Magistrate Yang has come to Xi and calculated the situation clearly, and the others have been notified to submit payment. A portion is still being cleared.

Appeal to Approve Increased Tax on Northeast Soybean Oil 112

The local oil mill industry guild stated that they had seen reports that the tax rate for food products, including soybean oil, shipped from Northeast to Shanghai was originally set at 15% of the value. Recently, in order to stop dumping and manipulation in the Northeast and protect the industry and commerce of the southeastern provinces, the Ministry of Finance changed it to 30% of the value. The future of the industry was deeply reliant on this policy. However, they suddenly heard that someone was opposing it, vaguely stating that the Ministry of Finance had cancelled the previous order. In recent years, oil mills have sprung up in Shanghai, Hankou, Xichang, and other places, and the soybean oil produced is sufficient for people's food. Since the Japanese and puppet regimes in the Northeast have dumped cheap soybean oil into the interior, the market supply has exceeded demand, and the inland oil mills have been greatly affected. If the order to increase taxes is cancelled again, it will inevitably be completely destroyed by the Japanese and puppet regimes. Therefore, yesterday they specially sent a letter to the county chamber of commerce, requesting them to telegraph the National Government, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance to maintain the original order to increase taxes on Northeast soybean oil in order to protect industry and commerce.

Land Price Declaration Deadline 113

The declaration of urban land prices in Wuxi has been open for more than six months. It has been extended twice, and yesterday was the final deadline. At 6 p.m., the declaration was officially closed. The township chiefs of various towns in the city assisted in guiding and instructing people these past few days. The number of households that declared their land prices has reached about 80%. The Land Price Declaration Office has begun preparing to carry out the work that needs to be done after the declaration is completed. The declaration forms filled out by the property owners will be sorted by town and township and used to write a public notice. The notice will be posted in front of the county government and various township offices for one month. If there are any objections to the land rights during the public notice period, the interested parties can file a lawsuit with the court. After the trial results are available, the winning party will notify the Land Price Declaration Office to include the land in the land price register. If no one raises an objection during the public notice period, the property rights will be determined and the land will be included in the land price register. In addition, if there are any fraudulent declarations, they will be handled according to the law. If the property rights are determined, it will be very difficult to make corrections. Furthermore, Article 10 of the Provincial Land Price Declaration Regulations stipulates that anyone who has obtained rights other than ownership (surface rights, easements, perpetual tenancy rights, pawn rights, mortgage rights) should obtain a list from the office and fill it out from today (the 16th) until the end of the public notice period.

Nantong Sea Bandits Burn and Loot Yuanzao 114

Yuanzao, a coastal area in Tong County, was suddenly invaded by a large number of sea bandits who looted the area and stole livestock, chickens, and ducks from nearby villages and towns. When they retreated, they set fire to civilian houses. The entire city was turned into scorched earth. Police and militia were dispatched to suppress the bandits, but they had already boarded their boats and sailed away.

Medical Students Dig Up Deng's Bones Case 115

Wang Shikuang, Sha Conggui, Huang Yiwen, Chen Dan, Yan Jialiu and other medical students from Nantong Medical University excavated graves and collected bones in the Yizhong of Duanjiaba in the south of the city to make skeletal specimens. The Public Security Bureau transferred the five students and the bones to the court on the evening of the 13th. After interrogation by the prosecutor's office, the five students were released on bail by the school.

Changzhou Kidnappers Demand Money Unsuccessfully, Tear Up Ticket 116

Yin Deying, a 56-year-old villager in Daqiao, Yiling Town, Sixth District, was wealthy in the area, which attracted the attention of bandits. At about 4 a.m. on October 26th, six or seven bandits, armed with knives and clubs, entered through the side door and searched extensively. Because they found nothing, they kidnapped Yin Zixiangdao (22 years old), took him away by boat, and fled east. Afterwards, Deying reported to the authorities for investigation, but no arrests were made. However, the Yin family was repeatedly contacted by kidnappers, but the negotiations failed due to the excessive demands. On the 11th, Xiangdao's aunt, Jiang, passed by Fuchenei, Zishu Village, and saw a floating corpse that resembled her nephew. She reported to Deying and hired someone to pull it ashore. Although the face was covered with knife wounds and blurred, it was confirmed to be Xiangdao. It was then learned that he had been torn up by the kidnappers. He was carried home, and the local prosecutor's office was asked to inspect the body. The office sent Inspector Meng on the morning of the 15th to inspect the body.

Another Bandit Arrested in the Hangzhou Daylight Robbery Case 117

Cao Chunlin, a bandit in the daylight robbery case at the home of Mao Chuxian, resident of No. 29 Wufu Building, Dafuqing Lane, Hangzhou, was arrested. A pistol and gold bracelets were found. He confessed to the crime. That night, the bandit, Jin Wang, and a five-year-old daughter were arrested in the Huayang Hotel in Chengzhan. On the night of the 14th, the Detective Team of the Public Security Bureau continued to arrest the criminal Xie Enpu at the Fengshan Hotel in Fengshanmen. He is currently under strict interrogation. All the bandits who are on the run will be rounded up to maintain local security.

Letter 118

Letter from Eurasia Aviation Corporation

To Whom It May Concern: According to today's newspaper, a Central News Agency dispatch from Kunping on the 14th stated that the Eurasia postal flight encountered fog and landed in the East China Sea, causing it to fail to arrive in Ping on the 13th. This news is untrue. The following facts can prove it to be a miscommunication: ㈠ Our company does not have a route through the East China Sea. The plane on the Ping-Yue route travels from Beijing to Guangzhou via Zhengzhou, Hankou, and Changsha, which is far from the East China Sea. ㈡ Our company's Ping-Yue route plane arrives in Beijing every Wednesday and Sunday, and should not arrive in Ping on the 13th. ㈢ Our company's first flight from Guangzhou to Beijing this week arrived in Ping on the 12th (Wednesday) on time and was not delayed. This matter concerns our company's reputation. Please investigate and correct the matter. The Eurasia Aviation Corporation Secretariat, December 15th.

Chairman Chiang Passed Through Shanghai Yesterday Afternoon 119

Arriving at Hongqiao at 2:00 PM by Sikorsky Aircraft

Then Transferring to a Ford Aircraft to Fly to Ningbo and Return to His Hometown

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek of the Military Affairs Commission attended the Fifth Plenary Session in Nanjing. Having completed his public affairs, he arrived in Shanghai yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM by a Sikorsky aircraft. He had lunch at Minister Kong's residence and rested briefly. Then, at 3:35 PM, accompanied by his wife, Madam Soong Mei-ling, he transferred to a Ford aircraft at Longhua Airport and flew to Ningbo, then took a car back to Fenghua to visit his ancestral home and rest briefly. He is expected to return to Nanjing soon. Details are as follows:

Strict Security 120

The news of Chairman Chiang's visit to Shanghai had been widely circulating in the city since the day before yesterday. The local authorities had assigned military and police to guard and protect the Hongqiao Airport. They were withdrawn only in the evening. Yesterday morning, there were reports that he would leave Nanjing at 8:00 AM and fly to Shanghai. After receiving the reports, the Municipal Security Department and the Public Security Bureau assigned many military and police to prepare for the visit. The Security Department, led by Wu Chuanxin, the Second Battalion Commander of the Second Regiment, deployed the First Battalion of the Special Security Team and a platoon of motorized vehicles. The Public Security Bureau, led by Tan Baoshou, the Chief Inspector, deployed a team of special police and a platoon of traffic police, along with the Security Team, distributed around the Hongqiao Airport, at the airport entrance, and at various intersections along Hongqiao Road and Daxi Road. Armed military police and traffic police were deployed to maintain strict security and direct traffic. Armed security teams patrolled along both sides of the roads.

Chairman Chiang is photographed flying to Ningbo (Photographed by Gong Shuxian)

Waiting at the Airport 121

Mayor Wu, Director Yang of the Security Department, Yang Yongtai, Secretary-General of the Military Headquarters, Madam Chiang, Madam Kong, and Soong Tzu-liang all arrived at Hongqiao Airport around 9:00 AM to welcome him. They waited until noon without any confirmed news. Madam Chiang and Madam Kong returned to their residences first, while the other dignitaries went to a villa in western Shanghai for lunch. After receiving confirmation that Chairman Chiang had departed from Nanjing by Sikorsky aircraft at 12:00 noon, they returned to the airport to welcome him. Madam Chiang and Madam Kong also rushed to the airport. Two bands from the Police Garrison Command and the Public Security Bureau were assigned to the airport and the entrance to the airport. Cheng Ziqing, the Chinese Inspector of the French Concession, also went to take care of matters.

Arrival Situation 122

The aircraft that Chiang arrived in was a Sikorsky amphibious aircraft, which he owned. It was piloted by pilot Smith. Normally, the journey only takes one and a half hours, but yesterday, due to uncertain weather and fog, it was delayed. The aircraft was not spotted until 2:05 PM coming from the northeast of the airport. In the blink of an eye, it reached the airport. After circling the airport once, it slowly landed from the southern sky at 2:10 PM. The dignitaries rushed forward to greet him. At 2:15 PM, Mr. and Mrs. Chiang returned to the Kong residence by car to rest and have lunch.

Mr. Chiang's Demeanor 123

Yesterday, Chiang was dressed in a dark blue camel hair robe, a black wool waistcoat, and a black wool overcoat, a gray wool hat, and black cloth shoes. He was dressed very plainly, and his spirits were quite high. However, Chiang looked thin and gaunt because he had been involved in the suppression of bandits over the years, which had taken a toll on his physical and mental health. In addition, he had nine diseased teeth extracted in Beijing and had not yet had dentures fitted. However, he was still in good spirits and greeted each of the welcomers. The only people who accompanied Chiang on the plane to Shanghai were his Chief of Staff, He Yun, and Secretary Wang Ruizhang, both of whom were also dressed plainly. This was because Chiang was advocating the New Life Movement and was taking the lead by setting an example.

Transfer to Ningbo 124

After Mr. and Mrs. Chiang arrived at the Kong residence, they had lunch. Mayor Wu, Secretary-General Yang Yongtai, and Yang Hu all went to the Kong residence to meet with him. At around 3:00 PM, Mr. Chiang and his wife left the Kong residence by car and went to Longhua Airport to transfer to a Ford aircraft to fly to Ningbo. Minister Kong Xiangxi, Mayor Wu, Yang Yongtai, Yang Hu, Soong Tzu-liang, and others accompanied him to Longhua Airport to see him off. At 3:20 PM, after arriving at the airport, Song Ziwen, a member of the Standing Committee of the National Economic Council, also rushed to the airport to see him off. Mr. and Mrs. Chiang exchanged a few words with the welcoming personnel and boarded the Ford aircraft with his secretary and chief of staff at 3:35 PM to leave Shanghai for Ningbo and return to Fenghua to sweep the tomb.

National Economic Council's Next Year's Budget Approved 125

12 Million Yuan Allocated for Water Conservancy and Other Development

Very Good Impression of the Plenary Session 126

National Economic Council Budget for Next Year 127

The National Economic Council held a standing committee meeting last Thursday evening at the private residence of President Wang in Nanjing. Except for Chairman Jiang, who did not attend due to toothache, Wang, Sun, Kong, and himself were all present. It was decided that the National Economic Council's budget for next year would be 12 million yuan, with 6 million yuan allocated for water conservancy development, 3 million yuan for road construction, and 3 million yuan for cotton, silk, and other expenses. The Ministry of Finance is responsible for planning this funding. If there is a shortfall, the National Economic Council will raise additional funds. Other resolutions were all about routine matters of the standing committee.

Sun Zhesheng, President of the Legislative Yuan, submitted his resignation to the central government, believing that the drafting of the constitution was complete and his major responsibilities could be considered finished. The central government, however, felt that there were still many important tasks awaiting Mr. Sun's completion, and therefore earnestly retained him. He also recently met with Liu Xiang, the pacification commissioner of Sichuan, and learned that Sichuan has vast mineral resources waiting to be developed. Preliminary Funding Methods Decided

No Result from Discussions on the Beiping-Hebei Boundary Demarcation

Railway Employees' Donation of Eight Aircraft Flew to Beijing Yesterday Afternoon 132

Naming Ceremony Held in Beijing Today

The eight Corsair biplane reconnaissance aircraft purchased from the Curtiss Company in the United States with donations from employees of state-owned railways were shipped from the United States to Shanghai. After assembly, they were test-flown twice at the Hongqiao Airport on the 13th and 14th and performed various combat flights, with good results. The aircraft were originally scheduled to fly to Beijing yesterday morning, but due to bad weather, it was delayed until 11:30 when they took off from Hongqiao Airport for Beijing under the command of Cai Chanfei, the captain of the Second Squadron of the Aviation Administration. It was expected that they would safely land at the Ming Palace Airport in Nanjing at about 1:00 in the afternoon to participate in the naming ceremony held in Beijing today, and then fly to the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo, Jinpu, Longhai, Jiaoji, PingSui, BeiNing, and Zhengtai railway lines to demonstrate and arouse the Chinese people's attention to the significance of aviation saving the country.

All sectors of the country donated salaries to purchase aircraft. Employees of state-owned railways directly under the Ministry of Railways enthusiastically donated a large amount of funds, reaching more than 920,000 yuan. Among them, the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways directly transferred a portion of their donations, 70,000 to 80,000 yuan, to the Aviation Construction Commission to purchase the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo No. 1 aircraft. The remaining donations from various railways were submitted to the Ministry of Railways one after another. The Ministry of Railways compiled the total amount of donations, totaling 833,882.06 yuan, together with the interest earned from deposits in the bank, 4,140.79 yuan, for a total principal and interest of 838,022.85 yuan, which was all submitted to the National Aviation Construction Commission for receipt. Subsequently, the Commission purchased ten new aircraft. All aircraft were named separately after the names of the donating railways. The names are recorded as follows: PingHan No. 1, PingHan No. 2, Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo No. 1, Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo No. 2, Jinpu, Zhengtai, BeiNing, Longhai, Jiaoji PingSui, Railway No. 1, Railway No. 2, totaling eleven aircraft. Among them, the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo No. 1 and PingHan Road Nos. 1 and 2 were purchased earlier and have already been named on their respective railways. This time, they will also fly to Beijing to participate. The remaining eight new aircraft are scheduled to hold a joint naming ceremony at the Ming Palace Airport in Beijing at 9:00 am on the 16th of this month. The Ministry of Railways and the Aviation Construction Commission and other agencies have jointly formed a preparatory committee to prepare everything and have invited the Central Party Headquarters and heads of various ministries and commissions, as well as public and private organizations, to attend the ceremony at that time, and the public is free to visit. As for the donating railways, the Ministry of Railways has telegraphed to designate representatives of staff and workers to come to Beijing. It is expected that there will be an unprecedentedly grand occasion at that time.

Shanghai International Settlement Volunteer Corps' Major Exercise This Morning 133

Participating Infantry Units Include Chinese, British, American, Japanese, German, Etc.

Anti-Aircraft, Light Artillery, Armored, and Machine Gun Units Also Deployed

According to the China News Agency, the Shanghai International Settlement Volunteer Corps will hold a major exercise to defend the Settlement at 6:30 this morning. The participating units include infantry from China, Britain, the United States, Japan, Russia, Germany, Scotland, Portugal, Denmark, Norway, Jewish, Philippine, and other countries, as well as anti-aircraft artillery, light artillery, armored vehicle, cavalry, engineering, transportation, logistics, and other special service teams, totaling more than 20 teams. The group has rented the second, third, eighth, and ninth courts of the First Special District Court as the temporary headquarters of the corps. The details are as follows:

Orders Issued Last Night for Preparation 134

This defense exercise is commanded by Colonel Graham, a British national, as the commander-in-chief, and Lieutenant Colonel Xu Tonghao, a Chinese national, as the deputy commander. Orders were issued last night to begin preparations. The Western District Command is led by Mr. Onstis, a British national, together with Chen Shixia, the commander of the Chinese team, leading five platoons of the Chinese team, two platoons of the British cavalry, and three platoons of the light artillery. The Northern District Command is led by Ivanov, a Russian national, together with Japanese nationals, leading eight platoons of the Russian infantry, two platoons of the Japanese infantry, and one team of armored vehicles. The Central District Command is led by Reto, a Portuguese national, leading the A team infantry, B team infantry, Scottish infantry, Jewish infantry, guarding the area south of the Suzhou Creek and bridges. The American infantry, German, Philippine, and other national infantry, plus anti-aircraft artillery, machine gun, and light artillery teams, are guarding the area north of the Suzhou Creek.

Reception for Chinese and Foreign Guests 135

According to Deputy Commander Xu Tonghao, the Shanghai International Settlement Volunteer Corps is holding this defense exercise purely for training purposes. The Chinese and foreign guests attending the observation include one representative from the municipal government, three representatives from the Municipal Public Security Bureau, three representatives from the Security Command, three representatives from the Songhu Garrison Command, and representatives from the Nanshi and Zhabei Defense Groups, who will be transported by three cars. On the foreign side, the British, American, German, and Japanese military forces have also sent officers to observe, who will be received by the captains of each team. They will depart at 8:00 am this morning and have a reunion banquet at the Shanghai Municipal Council International Settlement Volunteer Corps headquarters at 12:00 noon. The exercise will be conducted from 8:00 am to 12:30 pm this morning. Members will only carry guns and artillery, not ammunition. The exercise area will not be under martial law and will not interrupt traffic.

Imaginary Enemy Situations in Each District 136

Regarding the imaginary enemy situation for this major defense exercise, according to information from the corps headquarters, the Western District is assuming that bandits have been found in Huxi, Huangdu, Sijing, and Minhang, and the area is in a state of chaos. The headquarters received reconnaissance results at 3:00 am this morning (16th) confirming that there were signs of attack or intrusion towards this special area with strong combat capabilities. Their defense line is on Kaixuan Road, Fahua Road, Bailinan Road, Daxi Road, Hualun Road, Dunxin Road, and Luo Biegen Road. The imaginary enemy situation in the Northern District is found in Wusongjiang and Baoshan, with the defense line set up north of Hongkou, North Sichuan Road, Jielu, and Linping Road. The imaginary enemy situation in the Central District,

Page 14

is found in North Xizang Road, North Zhejiang Road, and North Henan Road, with the defense line along the Suzhou Creek.

Attack and Occupation Exercise 137

This reporter from the China News Agency obtained a copy of the exercise plan from the corps headquarters yesterday. It is specially translated as follows: (A) ㈠ During the exercise, members of each Volunteer Corps gather in the area designated by the order within each corps headquarters and listen to the commander's command. ㈡ In practice, the First Battalion occupies the area of the Second Battalion. ㈢ The Third Battalion begins to attack and occupy the Suzhou Creek at extremely speed, and after the First Battalion occupies the area of the Second Battalion, it retreats to the headquarters at extremely speed. ㈣ The Western District's surrounding group reconnaissance is carried out by one mobile team, including the cavalry and main infantry. The rest fill the First Battalion's replenishment team. ㈤ The Northern District's Hongkou area surrounding group reconnaissance is carried out by the Second Battalion's armored team and main infantry. ㈥ The transportation team practices handling transportation matters. ㈦ The traffic team practices relaying orders and reports between the headquarters and each team by telephone and delivering official documents by motorcycle.

Defense and Mobilization Exercise 138

(B) ㈠ Each unit automatically sets a password for vigilance and precaution in the first half of the night. ㈡ At 6:30, the commander-in-chief issues a password, using the words "Practice" (Paredes) to represent. ㈢ Gather at 8:00. ㈣ The infantry sets off to load transport supplies at the headquarters. These supplies do not affect the outcome of the exercise. After the headquarters checks the document box, medical box, stretcher, etc., the vehicles transport them to the assembly point of each team. As for military supplies, no matter how, they are transported by manpower or the traffic team. ㈤ The infantry assembles at the headquarters to perform various tasks, and the headquarters' logistics are supplied by the rotating headquarters. ㈥ The First Battalion, Second Battalion, Third Battalion, Armored Vehicle Team, and the five main teams each use motorcycles for the application of each team. ㈦ The headquarters staff performs internal work within the headquarters, such as creating report forms and military action maps.

Engineering Corps' Fortification Exercise 139

(C) ㈠ Each unit completes preparations and reports. The Cavalry Team is at the Racecourse. ㈡ The First Battalion is commanded by Onstis. The main defense is to defend all transportation roads, west along the Suzhou Creek and railway line, connecting Kaixuan Road, Fahua Road, and Aihe Road. The cavalry reconnaissance team is deployed on Hualun Road and advances to Luo Biegen Road, preparing personnel and supplies. ㈢ The First and Second Battalions occupy the destination, with the First Battalion on the right and the Second Battalion on the left. The Second Battalion notifies the First Battalion in advance to prepare to cross the Suzhou Creek. After receiving the notice, the First Battalion connects with the Second Battalion and rushes across the bridge to occupy the destination. ㈣ The Third Battalion prepares to occupy the Suzhou Creek, from the Waibaidu Bridge to the Xizang Road Bridge, but after the First and Second Battalions pass, it retreats to the headquarters at extremely speed. ㈤ The Second Battalion deploys traffic routes at the Bund to prepare for the advance and retreat of the Japanese team, while the armored vehicles also depart simultaneously to defend the alert locations, which are the unauthorized road constructions of North Sichuan Road, Linping Road, and Di Siwei Road. ㈥ The Engineering Corps works with the First and Second Battalions to build defensive works. In an emergency, they build defensive camps and electrical networks.

Central Bank

Reasons Why It Is Inconvenient to Re-Impose the Rayon Tax 141

Ministry of Finance's Reply to the National Products Factory Association

The Shanghai National Products Factory Association received a reply from the Ministry of Finance, Tax No. 3566, yesterday, "I have read your letter. The association proposes to re-impose a general tax on rayon blended fabrics to help the domestic silk industry. The theory is still correct, but the general tax is a factory output tax and should be collected on the factory's output. At present, there are no factories in the country that manufacture rayon, which does not comply with the principle of collecting the general tax. If we impose a general tax on woven products and determine the tax rate based on the rayon content, it is necessary to identify each blended fabric, which is very difficult. Even if we do not discuss it, most of the weaving of silk and all silk fabrics belongs to the household industry. After rayon is imported, it is dispersed to various places, and the weaving industry using rayon as raw material is extremely scattered and not concentrated. Investigation is even more difficult, and management is impossible. If we take care of one thing and lose sight of another, and there is more leakage than collection, it will still be of no help. The main reasons for the failure of China's silk industry are the reduction in overseas demand, the low price of silk, and the sharp decline in exports, not entirely due to the abundance of rayon and other products on the market. Moreover, the current rayon import tax rate is already above 60%, and the higher the tax rate, the more difficult it is to prevent smuggling and tax evasion. Therefore, merely discussing increasing taxes may still not be enough to protect the domestic silk export outlet. The request in the request is kept for reference."

This seriously hinders national tax revenue and affects the allocation of public funds to local areas. The accumulated old stamps are quite numerous, and safekeeping has been a considerable challenge. For the sake of prudence, the Chamber of Commerce, in accordance with the Ministry's regulations on registering old stamp tax tickets, will return the registered old stamp tax tickets first, pending the Ministry's instructions on exchange procedures. All merchants who have registered with the Chamber of Commerce can bring the vouchers issued by the Chamber of Commerce to claim their stamps. Those who have not yet registered should register with the Chamber of Commerce before the 31st of this month, and no further extensions will be granted.

(Explanation) It was decided at the shareholders' meeting in 1920 that 500,000 taels of silver from the factory's surplus profit would be allocated to the Sino-Belgian Shipping Company shares and 120,000 taels of silver to the second factory, with receipts issued to shareholders. However, due to various reasons, the shipping company could not be established. Eighty mu of land were purchased in Wusong in preparation for building a pier. At the shareholders' meeting in 1931, it was decided to reissue Dasheng Shipping deposit slips and to return the funds from the sale of the shipping land. In recent years, no one has purchased the land, and the company has not divested from its concurrent management.
