After repeated discussions by the board of directors, it was agreed that the relationship between the textile industry and the real estate is relatively weak, and it would be better to establish a separate company, with shareholders consisting of the factory and those who invested land as shares. A separate registration will be made, and a special commissioner will be appointed to manage everything. In the future, either the land will be sold, or it will be developed in another way. The proceeds will be distributed to the original shipping shareholders. The resolution was passed. The resolution was passed. ㈦ Re-election of supervisors. After counting the votes, Chen Guangfu, Fang Juchuan, and Yun Jishen were re-elected. The meeting adjourned at 5:30 PM.

Using Huge Donations as a Stepping Stone to Advancement

Zhang Shaolin Runs Schools to Collect Money 151

Huge Amounts of Money Not Donated, Actually Collecting Money Under False Pretenses

Affected Students Report the Situation One After Another

Public figures from all walks of life in the city, including Pan Gongzhan, Li Dachao, Wang Xiaoying, Lin Pengxia, Tao Xingzhi, He Bingsong, Huang Jingwan, Liu Renhang, Shen Jiucheng, and others, recognizing the difficulties of the nation and the decline of culture, believed that only through popular education could the nation's crisis be saved and the people's knowledge increased. This summer, they gathered comrades from all walks of life to launch the China Popular Education Promotion Association and establish schools, so that poor children would not be denied access to education. While preparations were underway, a man named Zhang Shaolin, residing at No. 25 Zhenxing Lane, Muer Ming Road, visited the preparatory office in July, expressed his sincere willingness to support the association, claiming to have a large inheritance and wishing to donate over 10,000 yuan to the association's fund. The initiators, thinking that Zhang was so enthusiastic about contributing money to promote education, considered him worthy of respect. As the matter was still in preparation and assistance was needed, the initiators unanimously elected him to handle the preparatory matters. However, after Zhang took office, his attitude changed abruptly, disregarding the importance of responsibility, and acting arbitrarily in everything. Furthermore, he took advantage of his position to advertise in the newspapers in August and September, recruiting free work-study students. The initiators believed that the recruitment of students had not been approved by the meeting, and that the association was still in the preparatory stage, not yet the time to recruit students. They immediately ordered a stop to the recruitment. However, Zhang ignored this and collected so-called uniform fees, book fees, badge fees, and apprenticeship fees from the students who came to register, creating various pretexts. The amount collected was not uniform, with some paying 40 yuan each, some 30 yuan, some 17 yuan, or 12 yuan, and the lowest being several yuan or one yuan, roughly based on the number of types of fees paid. The uniforms given to those who paid the uniform fee were extremely poor. The deceived students, suffering this unnecessary loss, could not remain silent and successively reported the situation through Fang, Zou, Zhang, Jiang, Lu, Tang, and others. The initiators of the association immediately conducted a secret investigation and obtained a great deal of evidence. Not only was it sufficient to prove that Zhang Shaolin was collecting money under the guise of running a school, but it was also discovered that Zhang was embezzling funds from the association. As for his so-called donation of inheritance, it was purely empty talk, nothing more than using it as a stepping stone to advancement. Now, the initiators believe that Zhang's fraudulent behavior has greatly affected their reputation and the association's cause and caused enormous losses. They find it difficult to forgive and have hired lawyer Sun Zuji to file a criminal self-accusation against Zhang in the First Special District Court, requesting that he be summoned for questioning in accordance with Article 366 of the Criminal Law. However, Zhang, knowing that he could not escape punishment, fled without a trace after learning of the accusation. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Liu Yugui opened the court. Because the defendant had not been summoned, the trial could not be opened. Only lawyer Sun presented the intent of the prosecution once, and Judge Liu ordered a postponement for further interrogation.

At 2:45 PM yesterday, a water heater exploded in Mingde Lane, Marlang Road, in the French Concession, causing a tragic incident with many casualties. Four people died on the spot, and eight were injured, who were sent to Renji and Guangci Hospitals for treatment. Three of them are in critical condition. The details are recorded below:

Subletting to Multiple Tenants 154

The city house at No. 177 Marlang Road in the French Concession is a two-story single-family storefront. The second landlord is Li A'jiao, a Ningbo native, 36 years old. Li's family lives upstairs, and the downstairs living room is sublet to others. There is a garage, but recently, because no car owner placed a car there, Li rented the downstairs to Guo Yongtai, a Yangzhou native, who opened a tin shop half a month ago. Furthermore, on the 25th of last month, he rented the pavilion room to Wang Guizhang, a Pudong native. Li also has fire insurance worth 1,500 yuan.

Dual-Purpose Water Heater 155

Wang Guizhang is in the rubber business and recently installed a water heater for heating due to the sudden cold weather, also using it as a boiler for boiling rubber, hoping to achieve both purposes in one fell swoop. However, yesterday, Wang burned the water heater until 2:45 PM. Because the fire was too strong and the water was insufficient, it suddenly exploded. With a loud bang, Wang's pavilion room completely collapsed, and the brick walls on the north, south, and east sides all collapsed, causing the pavilion rooms of the right-neighboring Jiang Gengji Western Clothing Store at No. 175 and the left-neighboring Yixu Noodles Shop opened by Wang Dalong (47 years old, a Yangzhou native) at No. 179 to collapse as well.

Explosion Results 156

After the water heater exploded, because there were many boxes of gasoline in the house, a fire broke out immediately. The nearby patrolman reported to the police station, which notified the fire brigade to rush to the scene to extinguish the fire and rescue people. The fire was extinguished after about an hour of pouring water. Upon inspection, it was found that four people were killed on the spot, including a male corpse resembling Wang's, Yang Wanxu (21 years old, a Yangzhou native), an apprentice at Guo Yongtai's tin shop, and Wu Gengsheng, a five-year-old child of Wu Yuanlang, a resident of No. 5 Mingde Lane from Anhui.

Investigation of the Injured 157

The seriously injured included Wang Guizhang (24 years old) with injuries all over his body, Fan Cunlin (12 years old) with a broken spine, Zhu Xiaodi (36 years old) with a head injury, and Wang Lianrong (58 years old) with a back injury. The above four were sent to Renji Hospital for treatment, but Wang Guizhang died in the hospital at 9:00 PM due to his injuries. In addition, there were five minor injuries who were sent to Guangci Hospital on Jin Shenfu Road for treatment.

Autopsy Today 158

After the tragedy occurred, the police station immediately sent a large number of detectives to quell the situation, investigated the truth of the incident, and summoned many nearby residents for questioning. All four corpses have been transported to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Funeral Home, waiting for the Second Special District Court to send personnel to conduct an autopsy today. At the intersection of Baker Road and Taiping Lane, the robbers urgently opened fire to resist arrest, and the police also fired back. The body was moved to the Feilun Road Autopsy Office. After questioning the deceased's aunt Wang Jingzhen and the maid Zhang Qiaoyun, Song announced that the deceased boy Huang Er'nan was indeed shot and killed. Public Works Department Traffic Committee Discusses Traffic on Hankou Road 159

As a Result of Hua Commissioner Xi Yushu's Strong Arguments

Cars Remain One-Way, Rickshaws Allowed

Since the implementation of one-way traffic on Hankou Road, it has had a significant impact on the market. Various businesses have closed and moved one after another, resulting in losses. The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, the Taxpayer's Chinese Association, and the Silk Industry Guild have repeatedly fought for its cancellation for four years, but to no avail. Yesterday (the 14th), the Public Works Department reopened the Traffic Committee to discuss the issue. Many Chinese and foreign commissioners attended. On the Chinese side, Hua Commissioner Xi Yushu represented them. The Public Works Department still strongly advocated one-way traffic, saying it was common practice in various cities around the world. The closure of silk shops was due to the depression in the Chinese silk industry and could not be attributed to the implementation of one-way traffic. Furthermore, according to the Donations Office, more shops have closed on Jiujiang Road than on Hankou Road, so it could not be used as a reason to cancel one-way traffic on Hankou Road. However, after Commissioner Xi Yushu repeatedly argued with reason, the decision was made to cancel one-way traffic for chartered cars and rickshaws. This is expected to be implemented soon. In fact, chartered cars and rickshaws have a greater impact on the business of shops than cars. Therefore, the market on Hankou Road is expected to return to its former prosperity.

Fortunately, the guards discovered it early and rescued him, sending him to Guangci Hospital for treatment. Now, while Zheng was detained in the detention center, he colluded with Liu Ruiting, a Yangzhou native and clerk of the detention center, to write a letter and attach a map of the detention center. He entrusted Liu to send the letter to Li Quangen, a local native and friend living at No. 16 Renji Road, Pudong, instructing him to prepare pistols, gunpowder, and strong acid in order to plan and implement a prison break. Unfortunately, the plan was leaked, and the French Concession Police discovered it, arresting Li Quangen, seizing the letter and map, and sending them to the Second Special Court for interrogation and detention. At the same time, the detention center was notified to transfer Zheng and the clerk Liu Ruiting to the prosecutor for investigation and prosecution. After the case was tried by Judge Qiu of the Preliminary Court, it was transferred to the Local Court due to the seriousness of the circumstances. The criminal court director Wang Gangxu conducted the trial. The prosecutor and the police lawyer filed a public prosecution against the three defendants for attempted escape, assisting escape, dereliction of duty, and bribery. Defendants Li Quangen and Zheng hired lawyers Shen Xingxia and Ding Yuanpu to defend them. It was declared that the proceedings were concluded and awaiting the verdict. The details have been previously reported. Yesterday was the date

for the pronouncement of the verdict. At 10:00 AM, Director Wang arrived at Criminal Court One, ordering the defendants to be brought to court. Li Quangen and Zheng Tangsheng were found not guilty. Liu Ruiting was sentenced to six months of imprisonment for assisting others in destroying evidence. During the appeal period, he was required to provide a guarantor worth 1,000 yuan. Zheng and Liu were returned to custody.

Continued Hearing of the Wu Hua Case 166

Defendants Not All Present, No Debate Opened

Head Office Representative Describes Liquidation Situation

The Shanghai Branch (No. 130 Ningbo Road) and the Eight Immortals Bridge Sub-branch (corner of Ma Gao Baolu Road and Avenue Joffre) of the Guangzhou Wu Hua Industrial Bank

suddenly announced their closure on August 21 of this year due to financial difficulties. The head office sent representatives Xu Yuangao, Huang Linsheng, and Yang Yigong to Shanghai to fully liquidate the assets. At the same time, ten depositors and current account holders of the branch, including Zhu Longgen and Luo Lihua, claimed that the branch had not been registered with the Ministry of Finance, had created false pretexts, used advertisements, and promised high interest rates to attract deposits, and had suddenly closed down, which constituted organized fraudulent behavior. They hired lawyers Zhang Shijie, Lou Yunmei, Xu Jie, and Mao Fengwu to file a lawsuit in the Criminal Court of the Second Special Court, accusing branch vice presidents Fan Shaoliang, Wang Jian'e, Ye Haitian, Wu Yousan, assistant managers Xie Shunzhi, Tang Songshan, and advisors Tang Shoumin and Chen Bingqian of fraud and breach of trust, requesting that they be prosecuted according to law. The case has been summoned twice. In addition to Chen Bingqian, who was recuperating in Mogan Mountain and was represented by a lawyer, the other defendants attended the hearing. It was necessary to summon the representatives sent by the head office for full liquidation, and the court ordered a postponement. The details have been reported previously. Yesterday was the date for the continuation of the hearing. At 10:00 AM, Judge Xiong Huiping and clerk Zheng Rongkai opened the trial in the Eighth Court. The plaintiffs and their respective lawyers were present. Except for Xie Shunzhi, Tang Songshan, and Tang Shoumin, the other defendants and their defense lawyers attended the court. First, the plaintiffs briefly stated the intent of the prosecution. The judge then summoned defendant Chen Bingqian to testify, stating that he was an advisor to the bank, did not know the reasons for the closure, and was unaware of the extent of the liquidation. Next, Huang Linsheng, the representative sent by the head office for full liquidation (Xu Yuangao and Yang Yigong were not present), was summoned. Huang stated that he was entrusted by the head office to liquidate the assets in Shanghai. After reviewing the accounts, it was found that the bank owed over 110,000 yuan to people, and owed more than 200,000 yuan to others. It was uncertain when the collection of debts could be completed. As for the liquidation of the accounts, they were working on it and would submit a report within two weeks for verification. At this point, the judge ruled that the defendants were not all present today and could not open the debate. He ordered that a new date be set for the hearing and that Huang Linsheng must submit the liquidation accounts for verification at the next hearing. The court was adjourned.

People's Postal Bureau Representatives Return to Shanghai from Petitioning in Beijing 167

Satisfactory Results from Petitioning the Central Government

Report on the Petitioning Process to Be Given Today

The Central Government, because the People's Postal Bureau affected postal revenue, had ordered them to close down within the year. Because the closure of the People's Postal Bureau would have a significant impact on the livelihoods of the employees, the local People's Postal Bureau elected representatives to petition the local authorities and sent representatives to Beijing to join representatives from various places to petition the Central Government. The results were satisfactory, and they returned to Shanghai by train last night. The details are recorded as follows:

Joint Petition of Representatives from Various Regions 168

Forty-nine private postal agencies in this city, represented by seven delegates including Qiu Zhensheng, Ren Shiting, Pan Wentian, Wang Dabao, Zhuang Gengtang, Hua Yunjin, and Qiu Yuantong, traveled to the capital on the 13th. They immediately joined forces with over 150 representatives from private postal agencies in Hankou, Wuxi, Tianjin, Suzhou, Zhengzhou, Gaoyou, Yangzhou, Shaobo, and other regions. Together, they submitted petitions to the Fifth Plenary Session, the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, and the Executive Yuan, unanimously requesting a five-year postponement of the closure of private postal agencies until a decision on how to handle the livelihoods of their employees is reached. Yesterday morning, they also petitioned the Ministry of Transportation, asking the authorities to consider their request.

Successful Outcome: Representatives Return to Shanghai 169

According to the person in charge of the local private postal industry association, the association has received a telegram from the petitioning representatives stating that the central government is extremely concerned about the livelihoods of the 100,000 private postal agency employees and has agreed to find a solution. All the representatives are satisfied and took a train back to Shanghai at 5 PM yesterday. Other representatives are also returning to their respective locations. The petitioning representatives from this city are scheduled to report the outcome of their petition to the entire private postal industry today.

Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau Responds to Ningbo Association 177

Increased Police Presence Every Morning

To Help Apprehend Wharf Thugs

The Shanghai Ningbo Compatriot Association reported that ships arriving from Ningbo often arrive early in the morning, leading to frequent incidents of hooligans robbing passengers in the Xiaodongmen area. The association requested the Municipal Police Bureau to take measures to protect the passengers. The bureau responded yesterday stating, "We have received your letter regarding women arriving at the wharf being robbed by hooligans near Xiaodongmen. We have been instructed to deploy police patrols in that area every morning to prevent such incidents. This is permissible because police service is continuous, and there is no rule against being on duty in the early morning. We have ordered the relevant branch bureau and police station to increase police patrols every morning. The detective squad will also dispatch personnel to assist in investigating the wharf area. This is to inform you for your information."

Domestic Goods Industry Concerned About the Issue of Free Gifts with Domestic Cigarettes 178

Domestic Goods Production and Sales Association Holds Meeting to Discuss

Regarding the government's ban on free gifts with cigarettes, the Domestic Goods Production and Sales Association reportedly discussed the matter at a meeting yesterday. The general sentiment was that while they should not object to the government's ban, the potential impact needs to be explored. The issue of free gifts may seem minor, but upon closer examination, it warrants discussion. The free gifts attached to cigarettes are mostly small industrial daily-use domestic goods. The monthly demand for these gifts is over one million yuan, and over ten million yuan annually. Many small industrial domestic goods manufacturers rely on this for their livelihood. Domestic cigarette manufacturers struggle to compete with foreign cigarette companies that have deep roots and strong financial resources. Therefore, they resort to offering free gifts as a way to promote sales in the market. With the end of the year approaching and financial conditions tight, a sudden ban on free gifts with cigarettes would directly affect the sales of domestic cigarettes and small industrial daily-use domestic goods, and indirectly affect the entire society. The association is concerned about the domestic goods industry and will reportedly convene a meeting of member tobacco factories to discuss submitting a petition to the authorities to temporarily postpone the ban.

Tobacco Exchange Association Urges Members to Register Stamps 179

The Shanghai South Branch of the Tobacco Exchange Association sent a letter to its members yesterday, stating: "We are writing to inform you that all previously used tax stamps held by your firms have already been reported to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for registration. Now that the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce has issued a letter and public notice regarding the procedures prescribed by the Ministry of Finance's regulations issued on November 8th, we must comply. This office has obtained and printed the regulations and distributed them to each firm. Many firms have applied to this office for assistance in obtaining application forms and registration slips from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and have registered accordingly. However, there are still many who are unfamiliar with the application procedures and have not registered. Given that the registration deadline is rapidly approaching, and we are deeply concerned that members may suffer losses due to missing the deadline, we are writing to remind you to investigate and comply with the regulations to avoid losses and facilitate closure."

The Coffin of Former Jiangyin County Magistrate Bao Sixin Is Transported Back to Baoshan 191

Bao Sixin, the former magistrate of Jiangyin County, passed away due to illness at his post last month. Three weeks have passed since then. His coffin was transported by waterway to Wusong the day before yesterday and temporarily docked. Yesterday at 1 PM, it was landed at the Tongxing Wharf in Wusong and moved back to Bao's ancestral home in Baoshan by his family members. Along the way, the Songbao Police Security Team and relatives escorted the coffin. In addition, various organizations such as the Baoshan County Government and the Wusong Chamber of Commerce, as well as local gentry, held memorial services at nine locations along the road. It is reported that Bao was only 36 years old, and he was competent in handling affairs. During his tenure of over ten months, he achieved remarkable political results. The people of Chengyi deeply mourned his unfortunate death, and they are currently planning to build a vagrant education and dining facility and a Sixin Hall to commemorate him.

Cao Mengyu Kills Daughter While Cleaning Gun 192

Ten-Year-Old Girl Dies Instantly

Cao Mengyu, a native of Anhui, is 32 years old and runs the Huada Pharmacy. He lives in a Western-style house at No. 48 Tinglifang, Tingli Road, French Concession. He owns a self-defense handgun. Yesterday at around 10 PM, Cao took out the handgun in his study to clean it. Unexpectedly, there was still a bullet in the barrel. The safety was accidentally released, and the bullet fired out of the barrel. At that time, his daughter, named Chen, was only ten years old and was studying at the table nearby. The bullet hit her in the waist, and she died instantly. Cao reported the incident to the police, and detectives rushed to the scene. They transported the body to Tongren Fuyuantang, and the detectives took Cao Mengyu into custody to handle the matter.

Mr. Lu Erkui, Editor-in-Chief of Ciyuan, Passes Away 193

Mr. Lu Erkui, a scholar of modern dictionary studies, previously served as the editor-in-chief of Ciyuan at the Commercial Press. He devoted himself wholeheartedly for many years and compiled the dictionary, which was widely popular in China and benefited countless students. However, Mr. Lu suffered an eye ailment as a result and retired at home. He relied on his son, the famous physician Lu Lusha, who took care of him wholeheartedly, allowing him to live out his natural life. On the 2nd of this month, he passed away due to waist cancer at his residence. At that time, his old friends such as Wu Zhihui and Xu Xiaotian considered Mr. Lu to be one of the few modern scholars and planned to initiate a memorial service. It is now scheduled to be held on the 23rd of this month at the Ningbo Fellow-Townsmen Association for a family memorial service.

Xing Zhigang's Request to Restore the Old Militia System 194

Xing Zhigang, the district head of the fifth district of Shanghai County, yesterday submitted a petition to the county government, requesting the restoration of the original county's local militia system. He humbly requested that the government, based on the situation, forward the request to the provincial authorities for approval in order to maintain local security. He stated that during the 38th district affairs meeting held on the 14th of this month, it was unanimously agreed that the county, in April, had reorganized the militia based on a provincial order. The order stipulated that the collected militia funds would be centrally managed by the county, and the original local volunteer militiamen would be disbanded and replaced with newly recruited local militia members who would be trained in rotation by the county. However, at that time, the villagers were in the midst of the busy farming season, and most were unable to respond to the call, leading to the recruitment of guest laborers to fill the ranks. Subsequently, due to the fact that the treatment was handled according to the conscription system, some local young men could not endure the hardship and dispersed. In October, the organization was again reorganized into the provincial security force, and its organizational structure became more cumbersome. This has distanced the force further and further from the purpose of protecting the local area, and all collected funds have been intercepted and allocated separately. A small number of militiamen are used to perfunctorily patrol the area. Since the beginning of winter, theft cases have occurred repeatedly, indicating that local security is not being maintained. With such a small number of militiamen, maintaining security is like trying to cover everything while missing key areas. Knowledgeable individuals have considered establishing watch posts, but there are no funds available to cover expenses such as oil and candles, leaving them with nothing but sighs and lamentations. The official investigation found that in the past five years, the district has relied on the local militia for effective protection, and there have been no theft alerts. Since the disbandment, theft cases have occurred frequently. Furthermore, according to the Pudong Star News, over one hundred cases of theft, kidnapping, and robbery have occurred in the neighboring Fengxian County in the past two months, which is truly shocking. Even in the Puxi area of this county, theft cases have been repeatedly discovered, indicating that the provincial security force is weak and unable to maintain security. Moreover, the local people believe that the responsibility for security rests with the provincial security force, and therefore neglect precautions, allowing bandits to run rampant without any restraint, which is a major problem for the local area. It is now proposed to earnestly request the county government to report the true situation of local decay to the provincial authorities and promptly issue an order to restore the original county's local militia system, returning the originally collected funds to allow for reorganization and defense of the area. These matters were recorded, and therefore, the official earnestly submits this petition to the higher authorities for review and approval, so as to comply with public sentiment and assist in public safety. The official would be immensely grateful.

### Eight Ruffians Convicted of Raping a Girl 195

Jiang Su'e, a girl from Changzhou residing at No. 24 Huai'an Li, Buck Road, was only fifteen years old. Due to her poor environment, her mother took her to various company playgrounds every night to entice customers. Around midnight on the 10th of this month, Jiang met eight customers, including Xu Tianbao, at the Tianyun Lou of Wing On Company. They went together to the Tongshang Hotel on Avenue Edward VII and opened room 138. In the middle of the night, Jiang cried out for help because she could not withstand the abuse of Xu and the others. Li Wenqing, a guest in the next room, heard her and felt indignant, so he reported to the police. Detective Ma Zhongrong and others were dispatched and arrested Xu and the other eight individuals, taking them to the Xinzha Police Station and sending them to the First Special Court for interrogation and detention. This has been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, the case was ready for sentencing. Judge Liu Yugui presided over the Eighth Criminal Court and announced the verdict: Xu Tianbao was sentenced to three years and six months of imprisonment for raping a girl under the age of sixteen; Chen Guixing, Tong Genfa, Li Wenyu, and Lin Jinwei were each sentenced to three months of imprisonment; Hong Renguan, Xia Minggen, and Yao Jinlin were all found not guilty. Zhang Tianyin, the lawyer for the police station, stated that he would file an appeal for the defendants found not guilty, and they were released in court.

### Publication of a New Book on Foreign Exchange Calculation Tables 199

丨Comparative Table of Chinese and Foreign Currency Exchange Rates丨

There have been few specialized books on foreign exchange calculation methods. Recently, Mr. Zhang Yazhuang of the Overseas Chinese Bank, based on his years of experience in exchange, compiled a book entitled "Comparative Table of Chinese and Foreign Currency Exchange Rates." The book has over three hundred pages and includes various comparative tables, such as English pounds converted to national currency, US dollars converted to national currency, French francs converted to national currency, German, Japanese, Dutch, Indian, Hong Kong, and Singaporean currencies converted to national currency, customs silver 0.715 converted to national currency, and national currency 0.715 converted to customs yuan. It also includes explanations, and the numbers have been carefully checked and are very accurate for exchange calculation purposes. The book has now been published, and the hardcover edition costs three yuan per copy. An additional five cents for postage is required for out-of-town purchases. (For out-of-town purchases, postage stamps can be used for amounts under 50 cents.) The Overseas Chinese Bank at No. 120 Jiujiang Road and the Dadong Bookstore at No. 310 Fuzhou Road are both selling the book.

### Publishing World 204

▲Chinese Typing Method to be Published Soon: The Chinese typewriter is a new invention in our country in the past ten years. Its effect can increase work efficiency, save time, and promote culture. ▲優游三元連中

▲Yoyo scored three goals in a row.

After the referee Marshall blew the whistle to start the game, Shaguer launched an attack, but was repelled by Yoyo. Mao Hongfa fired a shot towards the center, but Shen Shiqi failed to head it in, which was a pity. After ten minutes of melee, Zhong Tongseng dribbled the ball in swiftly and passed it into the center. Sun Jinshun rushed in from behind, raised his iron leg, and swept it fiercely at the goal, scoring in one fell swoop. In the twentieth minute, Mao Hongfa was blocked by Ke Xuemofu in front of the goal. Ke suddenly tripped over the ball, but it was just on the penalty line, so no penalty kick was awarded. Although Sun Jinshun's kick was powerful, it flew over the goalpost. At twenty-five minutes, Shaguer caused a disturbance in front of the goal. Tang Ji came out to defend, and Shaguer's ball bounced back off the goalpost, which was also dangerous. However, in the last two minutes of the first half, Mao Hongfa scored, making it two to zero.

▲沙谷頑强反抗

▲Shaguer fought back tenaciously.

Three minutes into the second half, Luo Haiguang received a ball from the right and headed it in, giving Yoyo a three-goal lead. Under Yoyo's intensified pressure, Sun Jinshun and Shen Shiqi each had a fierce shot, but unfortunately missed. After fifteen minutes, the Russians launched a full-scale attack. Goalkeeper Tang Shoumen was caught out of position while trying to deal with it, causing a mishap and allowing Na Shi Taiwen to score. Five minutes later, Loba Stowe swept the ball into the goal from twenty yards out on the left, with great speed and beauty, making it three to two. In the last ten minutes, although Sun Jinshun scored again, Mi Hailuofu also shot a long-range ball, which went over Tang Ji's head and into the net, resulting in a final score of four to three.

中央於盛怒之下、力圖反攻、希冀恢復城池故競爭形勢、益見緊張果由吾舜文攻入光華、球、打破鴨蛋紀綠、光華方與未艾、攻守嚴謹使中央健兒、屈居下風、奈何不得、最後光華蔣紹祥又中一球、成四比一之結果、明日上午中央將與曁南比賽、

Central, in a rage, tried to counterattack, hoping to recover its lost ground, making the competition even more intense. Wu Shunwen finally scored a goal for Guanghua, breaking the duck's egg record. Guanghua continued its momentum, and its strict offense and defense kept Central's players at a disadvantage. Finally, Jiang Shaoxiang of Guanghua scored another goal, making the final score 4-1. Tomorrow morning, Central will play Jinan.

西青籃球昨賽、滬中對民强一塲、因滬中往杭州作江浙私中比賽、故未舉行、將改期交鋒、乙組西青對俄僑、税專對軍官、曾有劇爭、結果西青以二十對十六反敗爲勝、税專則以兩分之差、倖勝麥令軍官、其餘各塲在一面倒之局勢中結束、最後一塲甲組賽、南星對同濟、賽來勢均力敵、比數極爲接近、開賽時同濟曾一度以六對二導先、入後南星左右逢源、一躍居前、同濟在後緊追、終無法挽回敗局、結果南星以七十七對四十三獲勝、今晚星期無比賽、

In yesterday's Xiqing basketball games, the match between Huzzhong and Minqiang was not held because Huzzhong went to Hangzhou for the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Private Middle School Games. It will be rescheduled. In Division B, there was fierce competition between Xiqing and the Russian community, and between the Tax Bureau and the military officers. In the end, Xiqing reversed its defeat to win 20-16, while the Tax Bureau narrowly defeated the Mailing military officers by two points. The other matches ended in one-sided situations. In the last Division A match, Nanxing vs. Tongji, the two sides were evenly matched and the score was very close. At the beginning of the game, Tongji once led 6-2, but later Nanxing took the lead. Tongji chased closely behind, but was unable to reverse the defeat. In the end, Nanxing won 77-43. There are no games tonight (Sunday).

市中心區越野賽跑 224

Cross-Country Race in the City Center 225

▲今晨十時在復旦起步

▲Starts at Fudan at 10 AM This Morning

飛馬越野隊主辦之市中心區越野賽、准今晨十時、在復旦大學門前起步、經翔殷路·淞滬路·三民路·府前右路·府前左路·府南左路·翔殷路·回復旦大學内體育館前終點、計程五英里又十分之六、約合八千五百公尺、沿途有公安局警士及童子軍維持秩序、石灰綫指示路徑徑、參加者共有晨光·華光甲乙組·虹口·滬西·飛馬甲乙組等七隊、健將七十人、如王正林·金仲康·楊慶燹·張良·方德忠·管友文·萬金生·徐彦博·邵亞俊·等、均著名長跑能將、集海上之勇將、萃全滬之精華、逐鹿於氣象一新之市中心區、平坦寛滑之柏油路上、爭冠軍於巍巍市府大厦之前、毛腿齊飛、人頭擁擠、將見江灣道上定有一番熱閙、比賽後、在復旦大學體育館内發給獎品、實可謂海上越野界之盛舉、

The city center cross-country race organized by the Pegasus Cross-Country Team will start at 10 AM this morning in front of Fudan University, passing through Xiangyin Road, Songhu Road, Sanmin Road, Right Front Government Road, Left Front Government Road, Left South Government Road, Xiangyin Road, and ending in front of the gymnasium inside Fudan University, a distance of five and six-tenths miles, about 8,500 meters. Police officers from the Public Security Bureau and Boy Scouts will maintain order along the route, and lime lines will indicate the path. There are seven participating teams, including Chenguang, Huaguang A and B, Hongkou, Huxi, and Pegasus A and B, with seventy athletes. Famous long-distance runners such as Wang Zhenglin, Jin Zhongkang, Yang Qingxian, Zhang Liang, Fang Dezhong, Guan Youwen, Wan Jinsheng, Xu Yanbo, Shao Yajun, etc., are all gathered, representing the best athletes in Shanghai, competing in the newly renovated city center on flat, smooth asphalt roads, vying for the championship in front of the towering city government building. With swift legs and crowded heads, Jiangwan Road will surely be a bustling scene. After the race, prizes will be awarded inside the Fudan University Gymnasium, truly a grand event in the Shanghai cross-country scene.

Ministry of Education Explanatory Compendium of Laws and Regulations 230

Two cases from the Ministry of Education regarding the interpretation of education laws and regulations: ㈠ Regarding the inquiry from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education about whether current teachers and staff of private schools can concurrently serve as school board members, the directive stated that current teachers and staff of private schools may also concurrently serve as school board members of their schools. However, according to Article 19 of the Revised Regulations for Private Schools, the school board bears financial responsibility for the school and should appoint more people from outside the school to participate. ㈡ A reply to the Hubei Provincial Government stated: Approved the inquiry from the Provincial Department of Education, based on the request from the Education Commissioner of Western Hubei regarding the naming, establishment, and jurisdiction of joint elementary schools of two counties, requesting verification and reply. Approved. Upon investigation, the expenses of the joint elementary school of the two counties are derived from both counties, so it should be named "Joint Elementary School of XX and XX Counties." The jurisdiction, such as supervision and guidance, should be presided over by the county government whose seat is closer to the school. Regarding important matters of the school, such as expansion, closure, appointment and dismissal of the principal, handling of school property, and budget review, it should still be handled through consultation between the educational administrative organs of the two counties in accordance with Article 1 of the General Outline for the Organization of Joint Primary and Secondary School Boards, etc.

丨First Individual: Dong Meili of Shanghai University丨

▲Second: Cheng Jin of Ginling Women's University; Third: Cheng William of Jiaotong University ▲First Team: Shanghai University; Second: Ginling Women's University; Third: Jiaotong University ▲English Speech Contest to be Held Tomorrow at 1:30 PM The East China Universities Mandarin Speech Contest was held yesterday afternoon at 1:30 PM at Shanghai University. Twenty representatives from ten schools participated, and the event concluded around 5 PM. The English speech contest is scheduled to be held tomorrow at 1:30 PM, also at Shanghai University. Details of yesterday's event are recorded as follows: ▲Representative Meeting Yesterday morning, a general meeting of representatives from various schools was held, chaired by Wan Guozheng of Shanghai University. Applications received after the deadline would participate in the competition starting from the next session. ㈢ The order of the competition was drawn. ㈣ Prizes were distributed. ㈤ Gui Zhongshu, Zhu Shaoping, Kuang Fuzhuo, and Wu Kaisheng were hired as judges for the English speech contest. ▲Speakers from Various Schools The speakers from various schools who participated in the Mandarin speech contest were as follows: Shanghai University: Dong Meili, Sun Shuhan; Ginling University: Jin Yanghao, Huang Niantian; Ginling Women's University: Tang Yiwen, Cheng Jin; Aurora University: Tan Weihan, She Yizhuan; Fudan University: Chen Qihan, Pi Yu; Jiaotong University: Cheng William, Zhou Shizheng; Business School: Shen Ruchen, Hu Mingxian; Central University: Zhou Shukai, Zou Zhenhua; Southeast University: Wu Qionghua, Hu Haiyu; Jinan University: Shen Yiwei, Chang Zhongbi. ▲Competition Situation The competition began at 1:30 PM. Fan Zhengkang was the chairman, and the judges were Jiang Jianbai, Pan Gongbi, He Bingsong, and Chen Xuanshan. After the chairman's report, speakers gave their speeches in the drawn order. Each speaker was allotted ten minutes. At nine minutes, the timekeeper would stand up to warn them. The judging criteria were divided into four categories: attitude, thought, voice, and structure, with a maximum of 25 points for each category. ▲Judging Results After all the speakers finished their speeches around 5 PM, the representatives averaged the scores given by the judges. The results were: First place: Dong Meili of Shanghai University, topic: "The Way Out for Chinese University Students"; Second place: Cheng Jin of Ginling Women's University, topic: "Youth and National Revival"; Third place: Cheng William of Jiaotong University, topic: "Reviving the Nation and Training Youth"; Fourth place: Zhou Shukai of Central University, topic: "The World in Extraordinary Times and China in Extraordinary Times"; Fifth place: Sun Liuhan of Shanghai University, topic: "Two Sick Man Countries." First place team: Shanghai University; Second place: Ginling Women's University; Third place: Jiaotong University. ▲Awarding of Prizes The prizes were awarded on the spot. First place individual received: Liu Zhanen's screen, Wang Qi's book, Zhang Shouxun's shield, Yang Jie's book; Second place received: Li Weiguo's shield, Chen Jianxiu's jewelry box, Yang Jie's book; Third place received: Mayor Wu's shield, Yang Jie's book, Li Shantang's inkstone box; Fourth place received: Lei Yan's screen, Yang Jie's book; Fifth place received: Tang Guozhen's screen, Yang Jie's book; First place team received: Luo Jialun's silver tripod; Second place received: Central College of Arts' shield, Zhang Jiong's calligraphy; Third place received: Yu Youren's scroll.

Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education Promotes Student Cleanliness and Neatness 235

▲Telegraphic Order to the Education Bureaus of Shanghai and Other Counties ▲Supervise and Order Students to Regularly Clean Their Homes The Shanghai County Education Bureau received a telegram from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education yesterday, stating: "Regarding the Provincial Government's Secret Order No. 2042, promoting cleanliness and neatness is one of the essences of the New Life Movement, and the implementation of this movement should be extended from individuals to families. Young students are the intellectual elements of the future and the backbone of society. This good habit should be cultivated as early as possible in order to invigorate the spirit and reverse the decadent customs. As the year is coming to an end, it should be stipulated that on the 22nd and 23rd of this month, all students over the age of ten should help with the tidying and cleaning of their homes, and have a half-day holiday on the afternoon of the 22nd. All schools should supervise and order students to comply, and must not be opportunistic, evasive, or perfunctory. In addition to providing early guidance to students on the methods of tidying and cleaning their homes, the principals and teachers of all schools may also go to inspect their achievements as much as possible the next day. Those with outstanding achievements may be given additional points in their year-end performance appraisal to encourage them. As the deadline is approaching and remote counties may not have enough time to issue instructions, we will first telegraph the order for implementation, so that there is sufficient time to prepare. This is the order." Accordingly, in addition to issuing separate telegraphic orders, we hereby telegraph you to earnestly comply and report the implementation situation.

Gold Market Breaks Through 60 Yuan Mark Again on Last Day of January Period 238

Swap Premium Increases Without Decrease

Resulting in Another Fall of 4 Yuan 3 Jiao

The gold market has been weak for consecutive days. The buying forces have been crumbling due to the influence of swaps to a miserable extent. Yesterday's market fell below the 960 Yuan mark because it was the last trading day of January. The selling pressure was overwhelming. Initially, the overseas silver market and the US market were flat. The forward silver price in Montevideo fluctuated. The exchange rate rose slightly. The price of London raw gold rose by half a penny. The off-market preliminary trading opened, and the bid was once 64.5 Yuan. Because the swap premium had already dropped to around 13.5 Yuan, the large short positions slightly added to their positions. However, the bulls were still panicked and closed their positions at high prices. Coupled with Juchang's vigorous selling efforts, the buying forces collapsed all at once, and the supply exceeded the demand, breaking through the 60 Yuan mark. The Central Bank's exchange rate was flat for both British and American currencies. The customs gold unit rose by one li. The standard gold price was quoted at 1005.8 Yuan. The market stabilized after the opening, struggling around 60 Yuan. Although the swap premium gradually increased afterward, the sellers temporarily watched from the sidelines due to the efforts of large players to purchase, and their power prevailed. Although the banks filled bills of exchange, the HSBC's exchange rate rose by 1.25 for British currency and 0.25 for American currency, which did not have a significant impact. ▲One-day plunge of several jiao to one yuan and four jiao

Yesterday, the market conditions at the Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange deteriorated further, and the selling pressure intensified. Financial circles said that new public bonds would be issued, so banks were selling off their existing bonds to prepare for the new public bonds. Retail investors became more and more restless, and market prices fell more and more sharply. However, if sellers stopped even slightly, market prices could easily soar, so be cautious.

After the second session, because the new buyers stopped, the old bulls closed many positions because the settlement was approaching, and the market for each month gradually fell. When the market opened in the afternoon, the trend of this month turned fixed, because the Tianjin gang still had a need for spot goods. It was heard that the warship called out 5 jiao and 4 fen, and 50,000 bags were traded by the artillery car, priced at 5 jiao and a half, but it still needs to be confirmed by telegram. As for the forward months, the market gradually fell because the factory also had hedge sales. The market in recent days has risen and fallen frequently, and the manufacturer's chips must be shifted to the fixed-price foreign wheat, otherwise, if the empty chips are scarce, the market will still turn stable. As a result, this month fell by 1 fen and 2.5 li, January fell by 2 fen, February fell by 1 fen and 7.5 li, March fell by 2 fen and 7.5 li, April fell by 2 fen and 7.5 li, and May fell by 2.5 fen.

Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

Prepare Quickly! Unite Quickly! 273

— Kang Jian'erfu

"The Flying General descends from the sky," is an ancient saying. Modern air warfare truly lives up to this saying.

Children! Do you know the dangers of aerial warfare? Do you know that the world's great powers are actively preparing for a second world war? Do you know that the "God of War" will soon grace us with his presence?

The facts are clearly before our eyes. According to the latest figures on military aircraft, France has 3,000, Soviet Russia has 2,800 to 3,000, the United States has 2,468, Japan has 1,600, and Italy and England each have 1,500. All of these are in preparation for the aerial warfare of the future.

Compared to twenty years ago, on the eve of the World War, the annual military expenditures of various countries have increased several times over. For example, Italy has increased by 26%; Germany has increased by 48%; the United States has increased by 190% (i.e., one and nine-tenths times); and Japan has increased by 388% (i.e., nearly four times).

Are these tense and imminent situations not a harbinger of the God of War's arrival?

Children! We who are born in this era, facing imminent disaster, must prepare quickly! Unite quickly!

Ford's Childhood Dream 274

— Lu Qiongyu

Mr. Ford, the American automobile tycoon, I presume you have all heard of him. Now, I am going to introduce to you his childhood dream that eventually came to fruition. I think you will all be delighted to hear it.

Ford started school at the age of six. Because he was very intelligent, he did very well in school. However, he always felt that merely studying books was uninteresting, and that it would be better to study something practical. Therefore, in his spare time, he would take apart clocks and study them carefully. After a year of such dedicated study, he had a clear understanding of the various components of a clock. In this way, he became a small clock repairman. After repairing clocks for a few years, he became a little tired of it and wanted to make his own clocks. At that time, he had already obtained his father's permission to work as an apprentice in a machine factory. At this time, in his spare time, he studied the machines for making clocks. As a result, he invented a new clock-making machine which, according to his calculations at the time, could produce hundreds of clocks per day. He was only seventeen years old at this time!

Dear children, I hope that you will also have the thoughts and aspirations of Mr. Ford. In this way, there will be a glimmer of hope for China's future.

Winter 275

— Azalea

The leaves are withered and fallen,

Having lost their autonomy,

Following a gust of wind,

They wail mournfully in the suburbs.

Oh, so winter has arrived!

The cold wind gradually becomes violent,

The temperature slowly drops,

Small insects cannot withstand the ravages of nature,

Some die, and those that remain hibernate.

Oh, so this is winter's revelation!

Winter has come,

The landscape is desolate;

Accompanied by heavy snowfall,

It chills everyone's heart.

But, harsh winter, harsh winter,

Under your oppression, our blood boils,

We are the children!

Aspire to Be an Aviator 276

— Dan Yun

Human transportation, in addition to land and water, has expanded to the air. The convenience and swiftness of airplanes and airships are truly beyond what people expected. Therefore, the 20th century is truly an era in which mankind has conquered the skies. Not only will future transportation be in the air, but military warfare will also shift from water and land to the air, because aerial warfare offers a greater assurance of victory.

The countries of Europe and America have a great interest in the aviation industry, so the development of the aviation industry is truly astonishing. Children! I believe you all know that on October 12th of this year, twenty aircraft from six countries competed in a long-distance flight of over 10,000 miles from London, England, to Newsham, Australia. As a result, an aircraft called the Comet won the championship in just 71 hours and 18 minutes, demonstrating their enthusiasm for the aviation industry.

If China wants to resist foreign aggression, it must expand its air force. Not long ago, everyone enthusiastically donated money to buy airplanes, which is a very gratifying thing. But I want to go one step further and hope that children will aspire to be aviators, so that they can serve the country in future wars with foreign countries.

With Good Hands, One Must Write Well 277

— Zhu Ming

American Judge Malone lost both of his hands early in his life. But since he became a judge, he needed to write to handle cases. Since he lost both hands, how could he write? For all records, he used his lips and teeth to hold a pen, and his writing was smooth and free. Within every sixty hours, he could handle more than four hundred cases. Isn't this exceptional! (See the copperplate illustration.)

Children, you are born with healthy hands, but often you do not know how to write well. Either the structure is uneven, or it is crooked and distorted. Of course, this is because you are young and still need to practice, but if you do not pay attention to practice regularly, you will never make progress in the future.

Since we are Chinese, of course we must know how to write Chinese characters; the more learned a person is, the better he can write.

Practice calligraphy is not much each day, as long as you are persistent, write a certain number of large characters and a certain number of small characters every day, or write large characters one day and small characters the next day. As the saying goes, "Calligraphy requires a hundred days of effort." As long as you continue every day without interruption, and persevere, there is no way you won't improve.

Malone lost both hands and had no choice but to use his lips and teeth to hold a pen to write. As for the method of holding the pen for writing, that is also very important. Briefly speaking, the thumb and index finger should be used to grip the pen tightly, the back of the hand should be round, and the palm of the hand should be empty, so that the writing has strength. I am telling you this in passing.

Stranger 278

— Gong Wang

There was a magician who, while preparing for his performance, felt the need for a child to help him, so he called his son over and told him what to do.

"Thomas! Be careful, you must not let people know that you are my son. You must pretend you don't know me, understand?" he warned his son.

"Understood, Father!" Thomas replied gently.

When the performance started, the magician asked, "Who would like to come up and help me?"

Thomas quickly climbed onto the stage! The magician turned around and said to him, "Very good! Are you willing to help me?"

"Yes!" said Thomas.

"Have you ever seen me before?" the magician asked.

"No! Father! I have never seen you before!" Thomas replied quickly.

(Note) Thomas is the name of a young child.

The Shoes Want to Eat Something 279

— Yi An

Crab 280

— He Gongchao

|| Its Development Process and Living Conditions ||

(1) Female crab laying eggs. (2) Larva hatched from the egg (magnified). (3) Slightly larger, resembling a shrimp. (4) The young crab only resembles its parents after its first molt. (5) The young crab's last molt. (6) Crabs feed on plants, fish, insects, and shellfish. (7) Crabs often fight fiercely with each other. (8) The defeated crab, having lost a claw, is able to regenerate it.

Children, have you eaten crabs in the past two or three months? Have you studied the species of crabs? Crabs can be found in both the sea and the rivers. River crabs often dig holes on the bank to live in. The female's abdomen is round, and the male's is pointed. The female's body and claws are smaller than the male's. The female crab digs a hole in the mud and sand and lays eggs inside, arranging the eggs with its hind legs and then covering them with mud and sand. After a while, the larvae hatch from the eggs, and they are very, very small. Gradually, they grow and resemble the shape of a shrimp. Only after their first molt do they resemble their parents. With each molt, their bodies grow larger. The molting process is like this: the original hard shell splits open from the back, and the new, soft crab emerges. Soon, it grows into a hard shell. Crabs often fight, breaking off each other's claws, but they will grow new ones. When you go to the river to catch crabs, if you only grab one of its legs, it will immediately detach that leg and quickly escape. Originally, its claws and legs are both easily detached and able to regenerate. Isn't this very interesting?

Little Brain Trust

Yellow Beans and Red Beans 281

— Yan Xinquan

Madam Shen, not knowing what to use them for, told a servant to measure out one liter of yellow beans and one liter of red beans; but the servant was careless and accidentally knocked over the measured yellow beans and red beans, mixing them together. Madam Shen was very angry and scolded the servant. Then she brought the yellow beans out and told Spring Brother, Summer Sister, Autumn Brother, and Winter Sister to separate them. Yellow beans go with yellow beans, and red beans go with red beans. So the four children worked together, the brothers picking out the yellow beans and the sisters picking out the red beans.

Mr. Shen, hearing his wife's scolding, hurriedly walked out of his study and asked what was happening. After his wife explained the reason, he ran around to the four children and saw that they were enthusiastically picking out the beans; two picking out the yellow ones and two picking out the red ones. Mr. Shen saw this and said, "You are too foolish. Why do you four have to pick out the yellow and red beans separately? If you four pick out the yellow beans at the same time, wouldn't the remaining beans be red beans? And you would save half the effort." The four children all agreed.

Winter Knowledge 282

— Gu Shengyang, Sixth Grade Student, Shou Zhen School

(1) Making Cold Hands Warm

Children! Winter is coming soon. In winter, your hands feel very cold. If you don't wear gloves when doing things, you can't withstand the cold. If you do wear gloves, your hands feel numb, which is very inconvenient. Therefore, in order to avoid these troubles, you can repeatedly rub your hands together before doing things. This will generate heat, and then you won't feel timid when working!

(2) Treating Chilblains

Children! Do you get chilblains in winter? This is a very painful thing. The simplest way to treat them is to soak cotton in kerosene and apply it as a bandage before going to bed. After a few days, you will surely be completely healed. If the skin has already rotted and the pain is unbearable, then grind rhubarb into a powder, mix it with water, and apply it. The pain will stop immediately.

Children of the World 283

— Wen Yuyang

(1) Poland is a newly emerging country in Europe. It was once a subjugated country. After the European war, they became independent and stopped being slaves to others, enjoying all freedoms. Therefore, their girls are also very happy, and practice dancing in their spare time. (2) Xinjiang is a province in western China. Their civilization cannot be compared to ours, so their dress is still the same as in ancient times. The children there have even fewer opportunities to study. They go to work as soon as the sun rises, and go to sleep as soon as the sun sets. Because education is not widespread, the government has gradually begun to pay attention to helping them.

(3) India has already been subjugated. Because they believe in Buddhism, they don't even care about their country. After the British invaded, some of them began to believe in Christianity. This girl is a Christian, and she is constantly asking God to prevent her from being a slave in a subjugated country, but this is also wishful thinking. (4) Java is a small island in the South Seas. It is a territory of the Netherlands. Their children live in a tropical area, so they are often naked and also like to dance.

Animal Curiosities 284

— Bing Yu

Animals' Food Consumption When we go to the zoo and see many strangely shaped animals, the things that these animals eat, speaking of tigers, leopards, lions, and elephants, which we have not seen, are truly astonishing. For example, the food consumption of a lion: every day it is fed seven or eight pounds of beef and horse meat, five or six pounds of milk, and one live rabbit. Every day it costs at least three yuan to feed it. Elephants are originally big eaters. Every day they eat thirty or forty pounds of sweet potatoes, three or four pounds of radishes, more than twenty pounds of straw, and five or six pounds of weeds. Their food costs more than five yuan. Polar bears eat one and a half pounds of fish and meat, two and a half pounds of bread, and two pounds of milk every day. It costs about one and a half yuan per day. Tigers and leopards eat the same food as lions, but the amount is slightly less, but it still costs about two yuan. Camels and polar bears are the opposite, they eat everything, such as wheat, grass, and salt, which are their main foods. They eat about fifteen pounds every day, but the food is not expensive, and it only costs two or three jiao to feed them. The food consumption of other animals, although there is more or less, fine or coarse, cannot be completely distinguished.

Animals' Lifespans The animal with the longest lifespan is the whale, which can live for 500 years. Next is the tortoise, which can live for 300 years. Carp and elephants can live for 200 years. Eagles and crocodiles can live for 160 years. Crows, ducks, and geese can live for 100 years. Doves and bears live for 50 years. Domestic ducks live for 44 years. Toads, cranes, and cuckoos live for 40 years. Lions live for 35 years. Horses live for 30 years. Cattle live for 25 years. Canaries live for 24 years. Cats live for 22 years. Earthworms and chickens live for 20 years. Rabbits, snails, and slugs live for 9 years. Chipmunks and mice live for 6 years. Fleas live for 90 days. Cicadas live for 40 days. Flies live for 8 days. Butterflies, from pupa to emergence, can live for 10 days. Mayflies only live for 5 hours. As for the lifespan of us humans, on average, we should be able to live to 50 years old. However, because of differences in local civilization, hygiene, disasters, and environment, there are also long and short lifespans. Before 30 years ago, Chinese people could live to an average of 45 years old. Since 30 years ago, they can only live to an average of 32 years old. This comes from the "Comparison Table of Lifespans of People in Various Countries" by a famous anthropologist. But if we investigate carefully, it is now rare to find people who can live to be over 80 years old. Among plants, pine, camphor, cedar, ginkgo (duck foot tree), cypress, fir, torreya, etc., can all live for more than a thousand years.
